- Figures to focus on: metric distributions vs error labels, before/after trajectory examples, and length/repetition statistics (to ensure PE is not merely shortening outputs).
- Claimed innovations: embedding-level, judge-free stability signals; explicitly optimizing process stability rather than only outcome correctness.65:T568,Distributionally Robust Token Optimization (DRTO) builds on Reinforced Token Optimization (RTO): a PPO-style actor update driven by a preference-learned token-wise reward. DRTO robustifies the actor loss via Distributionally Robust Optimization (DRO) by constructing an f-divergence ambiguity set over the empirical minibatch distribution and optimizing the worst-case (upper-bounded) token/trajectory-wise objective. The goal is to reduce sensitivity to minibatch randomness and reward perturbations, yielding more stable policy-gradient updates under distribution shift.

Key design choice: DRO is applied at the minibatch level (local ambiguity set per update) within an on-policy token-level RLHF pipeline.

Two practical instantiations:
1) KL-DRTO: KL-divergence ambiguity set leads to an entropic-risk / exponential-tilting objective, smoothly upweighting high-loss trajectories within the minibatch.
2) χ²-DRTO: χ²-divergence yields a tractable variance-sensitive surrogate, effectively combining minibatch mean loss with a standard-deviation-dependent term, encouraging both low average loss and low loss dispersion.

Compared to prior robust preference optimization (e.g., DrDPO, χ²-PO) that mainly targets offline preference learning, DRTO directly stabilizes on-policy token-level actor updates, while largely preserving RTO’s training pipeline and compute profile.66:T53c,【skim】
- Read the Introduction for the failure mode (small prompt shifts) and the main idea (DRO + token-level RLHF).
- Scan the contributions list to capture: minibatch-level DRO, two f-divergence realizations, low overhead.
- Check the main results figure (e.g., Figure 1) for the overall robustness gains under shifts.
- Skim the final forms of KL-DRTO and χ²-DRTO objectives to internalize the intuition: exponential tilting vs mean+std surrogate.

【must_read】
- Carefully read the DRO derivations:
  1) how the minibatch ambiguity set is defined;
  2) how f-divergence DRO duality yields trainable actor losses;
  3) how KL vs χ² changes the risk shape (smooth reweighting vs variance-sensitive bound).
- Study the integration with RTO: where DRTO modifies/wraps the PPO-style actor loss, and implications for gradient variance and stability.
- Scrutinize experimental protocols: how shifts are constructed, evaluation consistency, and fairness vs PPO/DPO/RTO/robust baselines (compute/data/hyperparameter budgets).
- Focus on ablations: ambiguity radius/temperature trade-offs, KL vs χ² by shift type, and conditions where robustness becomes overly conservative.
- Innovation checklist: first systematic minibatch-level DRO inside on-policy token-level RLHF; two drop-in actor-loss implementations with minimal overhead.67:T4c7,The paper presents the first targeted backdoor attack on pipeline parallelism, based on stage-wise task arithmetic injection.

Threat model: the model is split into N pipeline stages S_i across N nodes; the adversary controls an intermediate node n_a (a∈(1,N−2)), can only modify its local stage parameters, and cannot observe plaintext tokens.

Two-phase attack:
1) Offline phase (train a misaligned surrogate stage): starting from the same base model, freeze all stages except the controlled stage S_a and train S_a on a public unsafe dataset so that prompts containing a trigger (e.g., “SUDO”) elicit policy-violating detailed responses. Compute the stage task vector Δ_a = θ_backdoored[S_a] − θ_base[S_a].
2) Online phase (inject during SFT): during normal decentralised SFT, periodically merge the backdoor direction into the controlled stage: θ_SFT[S_a] ← θ_SFT[S_a] + w_a·Δ_a every fq_a steps. The scale w_a tunes the trade-off between stealth/clean performance and backdoor success.

Key property: no data poisoning is required; the attacker does not need full-model control. The backdoor is compressed into an additive parameter delta for a single stage, enabling stealthy, adjustable injection.68:T4c0,【skim】
- Read the Introduction to understand why PP differs from DP/federated settings and why prior PP poisoning is not targeted/stealthy.
- Jump to Figure 1 and Algorithm 1 to grasp the two-phase pipeline: offline Δ training + online periodic injection.
- Skim the main results: clean performance retention, trigger success rate, and persistence after safety alignment.

【must_read】
- Study the threat model carefully (intermediate stage control, no token visibility) and system assumptions (decentralised SFT with PP communication).
- Examine offline training details: dataset choice, how training only one stage can encode the trigger behavior, and trigger generalization.

- Focus on the post-hoc safety alignment experiment: why ~60% persistence remains and whether it correlates with where the backdoor is represented across layers/stages.

skim（泛读建议：方法概述 + 推荐看哪些部分）

- 最后扫一遍 compute/系统收益段落（分发体积、显存峰值），把结论与适用场景记下来。6a:T45c,They propose LottaLoRA: for each linear layer, use a fixed random matrix W_seed as the frozen backbone (the scaffold) and add a trainable low-rank update BA (B∈R^{d_out×r}, A∈R^{r×d_in}), with the usual LoRA scaling α and an additional trainable scalar β that scales the backbone contribution. Training updates only {A,B,β} while keeping W_seed fixed. The intuition is reservoir-like: a stable random backbone provides rich random features/dynamics, and the low-rank adapters act as a low-dimensional controller that steers computation layer-by-layer. Mechanistically, they report that when the scaffold is static, optimization keeps using it (learned β stays strictly positive, with architecture-dependent magnitude); if the scaffold is resampled during training (destroying stability), β is driven toward 0 and the adapters must carry essentially all task information. Thus, the exact random values are interchangeable, but being fixed is essential—linking the method to Reservoir Computing, with depth playing the role of “time” in feedforward nets and LoRA acting beyond a single linear readout.6b:T79a,must_read (deep technical analysis + what to focus on)
1) Introduction: internalize the “scaffolding vs task-signal” thesis and the connections to LoRA expressivity, intrinsic dimensionality, and Reservoir Computing; focus on Figure 1 (strategy comparison).
2) Method: carefully parse the per-layer parameterization (frozen W_seed, low-rank BA, the role of trainable β, α scaling, variance-matched random initialization). β is central to the mechanistic claims.
3) Mechanistic findings section(s): prioritize the key controls—static scaffold vs resampled scaffold—and track β’s sign/magnitude across architectures to understand when the backbone is actively exploited.
4) Experiments: follow the “small-to-large” progression; for each task, note the minimum rank r that matches full training (interpreted as an empirical intrinsic dimensionality estimate). If available, pay attention to layer-wise rank sensitivity/ablations.
5) Compute/system analysis (Section 6): read beyond parameter counts—check assumptions and the reported impacts on distribution size and peak memory.
Key contributions: (A) full random-and-frozen backbones can nearly match full training across many architectures; (B) β dynamics provide evidence that a static scaffold is actively used; (C) the minimal rank to reach the full-training ceiling serves as a practical proxy for task intrinsic dimensionality; (D) seed-defined backbones enable a distribution paradigm with quantified large-scale system gains.

skim (method overview + what to read)

- Briefly scan the compute/memory/distribution discussion for deployment implications.6c:T5bd,STACK (State-Aware Reasoning Compression with Knowledge Guidance) performs step-wise CoT compression by coupling state detection, adaptive decoding, and preference-style training:
1) Step-wise state detection: monitor local information entropy to detect hesitation/uncertainty; distinguish it from confident-but-overlong redundancy.
2) Dynamic strategy switching:
- Knowledge-guided compression: when uncertainty or potential bias is detected, retrieve external evidence (RAG) and apply contrastive decoding to steer generation toward evidence-supported shorter reasoning, aiming to both correct and compress.
- Self-prompted compression: when the model is confident but verbose, use self-prompting to remove repetitive or redundant steps while preserving the core logic.
3) Answer-distribution early stopping: stop further verification once the answer distribution converges, suppressing redundant self-check loops.
4) Online long–short contrastive sampling: treat the original chain as the long sample; generate a short sample online via step-wise segmentation and the above compression strategies.
5) Training: build on DPO-style contrastive preference learning while leveraging reward differences (highlighted as combining PPO-like reward modeling with lightweight DPO). The reward gap between long vs short chains drives policy updates, teaching the model state-conditioned optimal compression and using external evidence to mitigate bias under uncertain states.6d:T413,must_read (deep dive):
- Key sections: the STACK method pipeline (state detection → strategy switching → early stopping → online long–short construction → DPO-style training); the exact objective showing how reward differences enter the preference loss; how contrastive decoding is combined with retrieval.
- Key figures: Fig. 1 (taxonomy of prior compression: output vs model optimization), Fig. 2 (end-to-end STACK workflow and switching logic).
- Innovations to verify: (i) step-wise state modeling (not task-level), (ii) knowledge-guided compression for uncertain/biased states, (iii) answer-distribution convergence early stopping, (iv) online contrastive sampling + efficient preference optimization.

skim (high-level):
- Read first: Introduction (overthinking + bias amplification; why naive RAG gets dominated as CoT grows), the method overview paragraphs (two strategies and triggers), main result tables (accuracy vs length/latency), and the core ablations (removing knowledge guidance / early stopping / state detection).6e:T43c,RecaLLM addresses this by interleaving reasoning with explicit in-context retrieval:
1) Explicit recall spans: the model emits dedicated recall spans when needed, extracting relevant evidence verbatim from the provided context; retrieval becomes an observable action.
2) Context-aware constrained decoding: recall spans are constrained to be exact substrings from the context, ensuring faithful verbatim recall and making retrieval success automatically verifiable.
3) Task and data design: training covers cases from no-retrieval to multi-step retrieval; retrieval-intensive instances vary context length, evidence position, retrieval type (lexical/semantic), and distractor difficulty (random, hard lexical, hard semantic negatives).
4) Two-stage post-training: supervised cold start on teacher-annotated rollouts, followed by GRPO.
5) Fine-grained verifiable rewards: optimize not only final answer quality but also successful retrieval of known relevant evidence, providing stronger signals than outcome-only RL and directly countering retrieval degradation during long reasoning.6f:T459,The paper uses targeted weight pruning as a causal probe: identify a small set of parameters most responsible for harmful generations and remove them while preserving benign capabilities. Unlike activation/attribution methods that require choosing intervention sites and counterfactual activations, pruning is a direct parameter-level causal intervention. Main claims:
1) Compactness: harmful generation depends on an extremely small fraction of weights (~0.0005%).
2) Unified cross-domain mechanism: weights found from one harm category (e.g., malware) also control other harms (e.g., hate speech, physical harm instructions).
3) Alignment-induced compression/separation: aligned models show stronger separation between harm-generation weights and benign-capability weights than unaligned models; this separation strengthens with scale.
4) Generation vs knowledge dissociation: pruning disrupts producing harmful content, not recognizing/explaining harmfulness.
5) EM link: pruning substantially reduces emergent misalignment, even when pruning data come from a different harm domain than the fine-tuning domain.70:T83a,must_read (deep technical analysis + close-reading guide)
- Follow the causal chain: alignment brittleness → is harm unified? → pruning as causal probe → compact/unified/separable mechanism → EM explanation + intervention.

  2) Method: understand precisely how harmful weights are scored/selected, the pruning granularity, and how benign capability is protected/evaluated. Write down: the signal used to rank weights, constraints/selection to avoid capability loss, and evaluation protocol.
  3) Key figures/tables:

- Innovations:
  1) Elevating pruning into a mechanistic, causal interpretability tool;

  3) Proposing alignment-induced compression and connecting it to EM.

1) Drift: repeated refitting on finite corpora and regenerating/replacing documents induces finite-sample stochasticity akin to Wright–Fisher drift; without smoothing, rare forms are most fragile and can be lost permanently.
2) Selection: publication/ranking/verification/omission changes what becomes visible. The authors formalize this via lookahead: the effective public next-token law is the generator’s law conditioned on the continuation surviving an acceptance process (capturing verifier filtering, self-consistency selection, or search/CoT-like branch suppression).
They analyze long-run fixed points/equilibria: unfiltered reuse tends toward “shallow equilibria” where visible statistics can be matched without recovering deeper generative structure, while normative selection (rewarding quality/correctness/novelty) can preserve richer structure but may remove intermediate traces needed to learn process rather than outcomes.73:T73d,must_read (deep technical analysis + close-reading guide)

- Skim experimental setup + headline result figures to confirm training-time proxy fitting and gradient/alignment validation.75:T416,The authors propose the Spectral Sensitivity Theorem, modeling a deep Transformer as a discrete dynamical system and analyzing the accumulated context-sensitivity Jacobian J_L=∂h_L/∂c. Each layer propagator W_j=I+∂f_j/∂h_{j-1} is decomposed into a dominant rank-1 component plus a residual perturbation. Three geometric control parameters govern a phase transition: spectral gap ξ_j=σ2/σ1 (relative noise), alignment κ_j=v_{j+1}^T u_j (inter-layer coherence of dominant directions), and effective gain ρ_j=σ1|κ_j| (amplification/decay along the dominant path). Under small ξ and strong alignment, products of propagators are dominated by the rank-1 path. Theorem 1 yields two regimes: Regime I (Disintegration) when ρ<1, early context sensitivity decays exponentially (signal disperses); Regime II (Attractor) when ρ≥1 plus cumulative gain and injection-coherence conditions hold, the network enters a compression-seeking attractor where internal priors dominate and suppress acoustic evidence, manifesting as rank-1 collapse.76:T47d,must_read (deep dive)

skim（泛读建议：方法概述 + 推荐看哪些部分）

- 最后看实验主表与成本对比：确认在视觉与LLM任务上是否同时成立。78:T493,The paper proposes the Evidential Transformation Network (ETN), a lightweight post-hoc module operating in logit space. Given logits z from a frozen (or mostly frozen) pretrained model, ETN predicts sample-dependent affine transformation parameters (scales/shifts) to produce transformed logits z'. These are then interpreted/mapped as Dirichlet parameters α (evidence) to obtain a second-order distribution over class probabilities. Key ideas:
1) Minimal disturbance: adapt only in logit space to avoid overfitting and representation drift when only a small adaptation set is available.
2) Beyond Platt scaling: instead of a single global temperature/scale, ETN uses input-dependent transformation, enabling per-sample control of Dirichlet concentration (how much evidence the model has).
3) EDL-style uncertainty: Dirichlet mean gives the prediction while concentration captures uncertainty; inference remains a single forward pass (base model + tiny ETN), with no MC sampling or ensembles.
4) Training: only ETN is trained on a small dataset to encourage high evidence on confident/correct cases and low evidence on ambiguous/shifted cases, while preserving accuracy.79:T658,must_read (deep technical pass + what to focus on)
- Sections to focus:
  1) Introduction: the deployment-driven motivation; “logit-space minimal perturbation”; why sample-dependent scaling matters.
  2) Background: EDL/Subjective Logic ↔ Dirichlet; what concentration means; how prior EDL variants address overconfidence/shift.
  3) Preliminaries/Problem: notation (θ=ϕ∘h, logits z, Dirichlet α) and the exact post-hoc conversion objective.
  4) Method details: ETN parameterization (per-class vs shared, constraints/regularization), logits→α mapping ensuring positivity and stability.
  5) Experiments: main comparison tables and OOD/selective prediction plots to verify gains come from better calibration vs better separability.
- Figures/tables:
  - The pipeline overview figure (often Fig. 1): where ETN sits and why inference stays cheap.
  - The main results table combining calibration/OOD/cost.
- Innovation checklist:
  1) Post-hoc conversion of pretrained predictors into evidential (Dirichlet) models;
  2) Sample-adaptive affine logit transformation (generalizing static temperature scaling);
  3) Small-data adaptation with minimal accuracy loss and low runtime overhead.

skim (high-level pass)
- Read the first ~2 pages of the Introduction for motivation and positioning.
- Skim the EDL background just enough to remember: “output α → Dirichlet uncertainty in one pass.”
- Jump to the method overview figure and ETN definition: inputs/outputs and how α is produced.
- Finish with the main results table and cost comparison to confirm the practical advantage across vision and LLM tasks.7a:T645,Loom is a looped Transformer computer:
1) State: the entire machine state is a fixed-size matrix X∈R^{d×n}. Columns represent locations (scratchpad, data memory, instruction memory). Mutable state is stored in bipolar {-1,+1} encoding to enable exact threshold gating with ReLUs.
2) Execution: an 8-layer Transformer implements one instruction per forward pass; the model is applied iteratively until the program counter reaches column 0. Attention is unmasked; a high softmax temperature (λ=10) approximates hard argmax selection for fetch/addressing.
3) Analytical weights: all Q/K/V and FFN weights are set analytically; no learning. Several layers are pure FFN (Q=K=V=0) for deterministic arithmetic/correction.
4) ISA expansion: extends from “10 layers for 1 opcode (SUBLEQ)” to “22 opcodes in 8 layers” via opcode-as-operand-routing: many opcodes reduce to operand preparation/routing for a shared subtract core, avoiding per-opcode execution layers.
5) Layer fusion: introduces single-layer direct subtraction (replacing a classical 3-layer approach), merges branch-flag computation with PC increment, and folds scratchpad correction into indirect-access logic to reduce depth.
6) STORE and indirect write: adds STORE to support indirect memory writes. Using L2 address rewriting (FFN overwrites the write-address field in scratchpad) redirects later write attention to the dereferenced target, eliminating O(m) dispatch trees for variable-index array writes.
7) Compiler: a C-subset compiler targets the ISA (Python + JavaScript), enabling offline and in-browser compilation/execution.7b:T623,must_read (deep technical pass)
- Build the full mental model:
  1) Introduction: focus on the three headline contributions—22 opcodes in 8 layers, opcode-as-operand-routing, and STORE-driven code-size reduction.
  2) Architecture: study the X layout, unmasked near-argmax attention, and why Q=K symmetry is used for matching (e.g., PC to instruction position encodings). Map each layer to a micro-architectural role.
  3) State Layout: essential for reproduction; align bit-widths (ℓ=log2 n, integer precision N) and row partitions (PC bits, operand addresses, flags, etc.).
- Key items to scrutinize:
  - The 8-layer pipeline breakdown (if provided): fetch/decode/routing/indirect access/subtract/writeback/PC update/correction.
  - STORE + L2 address rewriting mechanism: understand how it turns variable-index writes from O(m) branching into O(1)-like sequences.
  - Single-layer subtraction via ReLU threshold patterns: core analytical arithmetic trick.
- Innovation checklist:
  1) 22-opcode ISA in 8 analytically weighted layers;
  2) Operand-routing to share a subtract core;
  3) Depth reduction via direct subtraction and control-flow fusion;
  4) STORE + address rewriting for major code-size savings;
  5) C compiler + in-browser execution;
  6) FPGA implementation with argmax attention.

skim (high-level pass)
- Read Introduction + first part of Architecture: fixed X, 8 layers = one step, loop until PC=0.
- Skim the opcode-as-operand-routing and STORE motivation sections.
- Jump to the demos/instruction counts and FPGA section for practical impact.7c:T548,1) A classification error scaling law: for supervised classification on a d-dimensional input domain with m classes and D samples, the misclassification probability scales as a power law in m, of the form ~ m^{2/d} D^{-1/d}. The derivation uses smoothness (a Lipschitz bound on p(y|x)) and a nearest-same-label sample argument to upper-bound error.
2) Decomposition as a tree of smaller classifications: the original large m_total-way decision is decomposed into L sequential decisions, each an m_step-way classification; this forms a tree where CoT corresponds to traversing a path that progressively narrows the answer space.
3) Optimal branching factor and a “thinking threshold”: under a fixed total number of classes (equivalently, fixed leaf count / distinguishable answers), error is minimized by a balanced tree with an optimal per-step degree m* = e^{d/2}. If the per-step degree m_step < m*, increasing depth (longer CoT / more steps) worsens error; if m_step > m*, increasing depth reduces error up to a finite optimal depth, after which further depth cannot beat a minimum achievable error.
4) Reconciling conflicting observations: “overthinking hurts” and “long CoT can still work” are consistent—what matters is whether each step carries enough information (degree above threshold) and whether the decomposition is balanced.7d:T6b4,must_read (deep dive)
- Key sections:
  1) The section deriving the power-law scaling of classification error: focus on how Lipschitz smoothness and nearest same-class sample distance yield the ~ m^{2/d} D^{-1/d} dependence, and how intrinsic dimension d enters.
  2) The decomposition/tree analysis: understand how “fixed total classes” is formalized as a constraint on leaf count, how errors compose along depth, and why the balanced tree is optimal.
  3) The “thinking threshold” result: track the conditions leading to m* = e^{d/2}, why depth hurts when m_step < m*, why it helps (then saturates) when m_step > m*, and the argument for an irreducible minimum error.
- Figures/tables to prioritize (if present in the full paper):
  - log-log plots of error vs number of classes m;
  - phase diagrams/heatmaps of error vs depth for different degrees under fixed total classes;
  - curves showing m* as a function of d.
- Innovation checklist:
  - formalizing CoT as tree-structured decomposition of a large classification;
  - deriving an optimal branching factor m* and a threshold criterion for when “thinking” helps vs hurts;
  - using a single scaling-law lens to explain optimal reasoning length and the importance of structure.

skim (high-level)
- Read the Introduction for the setup (classification view, CoT as a tree, thinking as deeper trees) and the three headline results (power law, optimal degree, threshold + saturation).
- Skim the assumptions behind the scaling law (uniform class frequency, Lipschitz smoothness, intrinsic dimension d) and the final formula.
- Jump to the decomposition conclusions/discussion mapping the theory to CoT length, structured reasoning, and overthinking.7e:T536,1) Benchmark construction (HiL-Bench): starting from SWE-Bench Pro and BIRD tasks, the authors select items that top models can solve with high success when full context is restored, then inject 3–5 human-validated blockers (missing info, ambiguity, contradictions). Hidden information is stored in a blocker registry.
2) Interaction mechanism: agents get an ask_human() tool acting as an oracle; it returns information only when the question precisely targets a registered blocker, making question quality measurable.
3) Progressive discovery: blockers are designed to surface during execution and environment exploration rather than upfront inspection, forcing an iterative loop (work → hit a gap → ask → continue) and preventing degenerate “ask everything at the start” strategies.
4) Metrics: besides pass rate, the benchmark introduces Ask-F1 (harmonic mean of question precision and blocker recall) to penalize question spam while rewarding targeted escalation. Tasks are designed so they cannot be passed without resolving all blockers, tightly coupling recall to outcome.
5) Analysis and training: the paper provides a multi-dimensional failure taxonomy showing model-family-specific judgment signatures, and demonstrates trainability via RLVR with Ask-F1-shaped rewards improving recall, precision, and pass rate.7f:T549,must_read (deep dive)

  4) Ask-F1: why F1 (precision/recall tradeoff) is hard to game and how it ties process to outcome.
  5) Failure taxonomy + RLVR: evidence of structural differences across model families and how reward shaping changes behavior.

skim (high-level)

- Check the main results tables: gaps between pass rate and Ask-F1 across models, and whether RLVR improves both.80:T4b5,CORA frames safety as selective action execution (prediction with abstention). At each step, a base policy proposes an action a^t; a safety controller decides Execute vs Abstain.

CORA couples three components:
1) An action-conditional Guardian model Rψ that estimates the risk of executing the specific proposed action in the current GUI state/history.
2) A Conformal Calibration module using Conformal Risk Control (CRC) to calibrate the execute/abstain boundary to satisfy a user-specified risk budget α on the executed-harm rate (rather than thresholding raw scores). For deployment realism, it incorporates weighted calibration under covariate shift and conservative extensions for sequential dependence.
3) A trainable Diagnostician that handles rejected actions with minimal interventions—Confirm, Reflect, or Abort—to reduce harm while controlling user interruption.

Additionally, CORA uses Goal-Lock: it freezes the user goal and treats on-screen text as untrusted evidence to mitigate indirect prompt injection/goal hijacking.

Evaluation is reported as risk–coverage and safety–helpfulness–interruption frontiers, matching the real deployment trade-off between autonomy and Compiler","starred":false,"priority":"p3","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-09T19:13:15+00:00","category_id":"industry","cover_url":"/covers/2604_08720.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.SE","cs.AI"],"summary":{"core_problem":"论文聚焦于 PyTorch 编译器 torch.compile 中“正确性静默错误（correctness bugs）”：编译后的深度学习模型产生错误输出，但不抛异常、不崩溃、无告警，因而难以及时发现与定位。作者指出该类问题在 PyTorch 社区高优先级 issue 中占比高（约 19.2%），且会直接破坏下游 LLM 训练/推理的可靠性（例如导致训练不收敛）。","importance":"torch.compile 已成为 LLM 训练与推理的关键性能基础设施（被 vLLM、AWS 等集成）。静默正确性错误的危害在于：1）不会触发传统监控信号（异常/崩溃），更容易进入生产；2）可能造成灾难性后果（医疗、金融、自动驾驶等高风险场景）；3）相较崩溃类 bug，更难通过常规 fuzz/崩溃导向测试发现。论文强调该问题在动态 Python/JIT 捕获图的编译架构下具有独特性，不能直接套用静态图编译器（TVM/Glow）上的经验。","technical_approach":"论文的技术路线分三步：\n1）实证研究与分类：收集并人工检查 116 个真实世界 torch.compile 正确性 bug，系统化归纳其“类型—子类—根因—触发模式”。作者总结三大类 bug：图相关（graph-related）、算子相关（operator-related）、内存相关（memory-related），并细分为 6 个子类；给出每个子类的典型根因与触发模式。一个关键发现是：in-place 操作处理 bug 占比最高（21.6%），常见根因是 torch.compile 内部对 aliasing（别名/共享存储）关系跟踪不正确。\n2）现有测试技术评测：选取 5 种 SOTA 深度学习编译器测试技术，构建基准并评估其对上述 116 个正确性 bug 的检出能力；并进一步分析“检出/漏检”的 bug 特征，定位方法缺口。\n3）面向触发模式的改进方法 AlignGuard：提出一个 proof-of-concept 的 LLM 驱动测试变异（test mutation）方法。核心思想是：以实证研究提炼的触发模式为“变异目标”，对现有测试用例进行定向变异，诱导 torch.compile 更可能进入错误路径，从而提升静默正确性 bug 的暴露概率。AlignGuard 最终发现 23 个此前未知的正确性 bug（均被确认，且已有部分修复）。","experiments":"实验与结果要点：\n- 数据集：116 个真实世界 torch.compile 正确性 bug（人工审阅与归因）。\n- 现有技术评测：5 种 SOTA 测试技术合计仅检出 33.8% 的正确性 bug，暴露出显著检测缺口。作者指出关键原因之一是：torch.compile 的正确性 bug 触发模式具有“动态/JIT 捕图 + Python 非计算语句/控制流/运行时行为”等特征，而现有方法的测试生成策略未覆盖这些模式；例如图相关 bug 往往由模型中的非计算操作触发，但现有技术未能覆盖，导致图相关 bug 全部漏检。\n- AlignGuard：基于触发模式定向变异，发现 23 个新 bug；其中 14/23 被标为高优先级；已确认且部分已被 PyTorch 开发者修复（文中提到已修复 10 个已报告 bug）。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读建议：详细技术分析路径）\n- 重点章节：\n  1）Introduction：把“静默正确性错误”的工程危害与社区数据（19.2%）讲清楚，并给出 OLMo 训练不收敛的动机案例（对应 Figure 1）。\n  2）实证研究方法与分类结果（论文中描述 116 个 bug 的收集/标注/分类、三大类六子类、根因与触发模式）：这是全文最核心的“知识蒸馏”部分，直接决定后续评测与 AlignGuard 的设计合理性。\n  3）SOTA 测试技术评测部分：关注基准构建方式、判定正确性的 oracle 设计、以及“为什么只能检出 33.8%”的归因分析（尤其是图相关 bug 全漏检的原因）。\n  4）AlignGuard 方法：精读其“触发模式 → 变异算子/提示词/约束 → 生成与筛选 → 差分验证（compiled vs eager）”的闭环；重点看它如何把经验分类转化为可执行的测试生成策略。\n- 重点图表/信息：\n  - Figure 1（或动机图）：展示正确性 bug 对训练收敛/性能的真实影响。\n  - bug 类型占比与子类分布（含 paper investigates “silent correctness bugs” in PyTorch’s compiler (torch.compile): compiled DL models produce wrong outputs without exceptions, crashes, or warnings, making them hard to detect and diagnose. The authors show this is a major practical issue—about 19.2% of high-priority PyTorch issues are incorrect outputs caused by torch.compile—and can severely harm LLM training/inference reliability (e.g., training non-convergence).","importance":"torch.compile is becoming a key performance layer for LLM systems (adopted by vLLM, AWS, etc.). Silent correctness bugs are particularly dangerous because (1) they evade traditional failure signals (no crash/exception), (2) they can propagate into production and high-stakes domains (medical/finance/autonomous driving), and (3) they are harder to uncover than crash bugs with conventional testing. The paper argues that torch.compile’s dynamic Python + JIT graph capture architecture yields distinct triggering patterns compared to static-graph compilers (e.g., TVM/Glow), so prior bug studies do not directly transfer.","technical_approach":"The work follows a three-stage approach:\n1) Empirical characterization: collect and manually inspect 116 real-world torch.compile correctness bugs; systematically derive bug “types → subtypes → root causes → triggering patterns.” They identify three main types—graph-related, operator-related, and memory-related—split into six subcategories, each with explicit root causes and triggers. A key finding is that in-place handling bugs are the most prevalent (21.6%), often rooted in incorrect aliasing tracking inside torch.compile.\n2) Evaluation of existing testing techniques: benchmark five state-of-the-art DL compiler testing techniques on the 116-bug set; analyze which bugs are detected vs missed to pinpoint capability gaps.\n3) AlignGuard: propose a proof-of-concept LLM-based test mutation method that injects the distilled triggering patterns into targeted mutations of existing tests, aiming to drive torch.compile into bug-triggering scenarios and expose silent wrong outputs via differential checking.","experiments":"Key experimental results:\n- Dataset: 116 real-world torch.compile silent correctness bugs (manually curated and categorized).\n- SOTA testing evaluation: the five selected techniques collectively detect only 33.8% of the bugs, revealing a large detection gap. A highlighted reason is missing domain-specific generation strategies for torch.compile’s unique triggers; e.g., graph-related bugs are often triggered by non-computational operations in Python/DL programs, which existing techniques do not cover—leading to zero detection for graph-related bugs.\n- AlignGuard: finds 23 previously unknown correctness bugs; all confirmed by PyTorch developers, with 10 reported bugs already fixed; 14/23 are labeled high-priority.","reading_guide":"$18","authors_note":"The authors’ central claim is that silent correctness bugs in torch.compile represent a systemic reliability risk tied to its dynamic Python/JIT graph-capture design, and existing DL compiler testing approaches have structural coverage gaps in this setting. discovery."},"reading_tier":"skim","recommendation":{"zh":"对训练infra很实用但别通读：只看他们对静默正确性bug的分类、触发模式与检测建议，能直接转成你们torch.compile回归测试与监控清单。","en":"Practical for training infra but not a full read: focus on MLP：由 P 棵深度 D 的完美二叉树并行组成。对每个 token 输入 x，每棵树从根到叶进行 D 次硬二分路由（每层只访问一个节点），因此每棵树仅激活一条 root-to-leaf 路径；整层总激活节点数固定为 P×D。每个节点同时包含：(1) routing 线性打分（w_in,b_in）产生标量 logit，用硬阈值/指示函数决定走左/右子树，并用 stop-gradient Transformers, FFN/MLP blocks dominate parameters and compute, becoming a major bottleneck at scale. MoE reduces per-token compute via dynamic sparsity but typically requires a separate router, load-balancing losses, and specialized infrastructure. This paper asks whether hard-routed, tree-structured feed-forward layers (FFF) can serve as drop-in replacements for MLPs in GPT-style autoregressive LMs, achieving very high conditional sparsity without a separate router while matching dense baselines, including at >1B parameters and in zero/few-shot downstream settings.","importance":"A practical alternative to MoE that activates <5% of FFN units per token while preserving LM and downstream performance would materially reduce training/inference cost and simplify deployment. Tree-structured sparsity is also more predictable/structured (entire subtrees can be skipped), which is attractive for compiler/kernel optimization. The discovered emergent auto-pruning suggests dynamic routing can naturally solidify into structural sparsity during training, potentially yielding additional runtime savings without explicit pruning or auxiliary regularization.","technical_approach":"$19","experiments":"The main controlled study trains 125M GPT-style LMs from scratch, comparing dense FFN, FFF, and sparsity-matched MoE (top-k=2) under the same training pipeline. FFF uses D=3/5/7 (≈75%/90%/97% sparsity). Training-loss curves (averaged over multiple seeds) show FFF matches sparsity-matched MoE closely, with negligible degradation even at 97% sparsity. The paper further reports scalability beyond 1B parameters and evaluations on downstream QA in zero/few-shot regimes with performance comparable to dense baselines. It also provides layer-level runtime benchmarks to quantify real efficiency trade-offs, and analyzes auto-pruning via utilization/routing-distribution dynamics and architectural ablations.","reading_guide":"$1a","authors_note":"The authors’ central claim is that hard-routed tree-structured FF layers can be a practical, scalable drop-in alternative to dense FFNs and MoE: they demonstrate (for the first time) applicability to autoregressive LMs and scaling beyond 1B parameters while matching dense baselines under controlled training/fine-tuning. NPUs","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-09T23:50:56+00:00","category_id":"llm_pretrain","cover_url":"/covers/2604_08826.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.LG","cs.AI","cs.CL"],"summary":{"core_problem":"大模型预训练受限于算力与显存带宽，低精度训练是关键路径。FP4（4-bit 浮点）可显著提升吞吐与降低带宽，但极低精度带来数值不稳定，尤其是梯度量化在存在 outlier 时会因 block scaling 由最大值主导而产生系统性偏置与大量下溢为 0，破坏反传与优化。本文要解决的问题是：在华为 Ascend NPU 上，HiFloat4（HiF4）这种分层缩放 FP4 格式能否实现端到端大规模 LLM 预训练，并相对 MXFP4 以更少的稳定化“辅助手段”获得更小的 loss gap 与更低的性能开销。","importance":"若能把训练中约 90% 的存储与计算放到 FP4，同时把相对全精度的损失差距控制在 ~1%–1.5%，就能在功耗受限的专用 NPU 上显著降低训练成本、提升能效，并推动更大模型/更多数据的可行性。更重要的是，论文比较了不同 FP4 格式在“需要多少额外高精度操作才能稳定训练”上的差异：这直接决定 FP4 方案的真实端到端加速是否能兑现。","technical_approach":"核心是围绕 Ascend NPU 的 FP4 预训练流水线设计与格式对比。\n(1) 数值格式：HiF4 采用三层分层缩放（hierarchical scaling），以 64 元素为块：顶层 scaler 用 E6M2，第二/三层用 E1，FP4 数值本体用 S1P2（等价 E1M2）。这种设计在极低 bit 下扩展动态范围并保留一定尾数精度，目标是降低量化误差与梯度偏置。\n(2) 稳定化算法：沿用近期 FP4 训练常用技巧——梯度量化用随机舍入（SR）降低偏置；反向计算权重梯度时用随机 Hadamard 变换（RHT）做去相关/摊平 outlier，减少某些维度主导缩放导致的下溢。\n(3) 关键对比点：作者强调 HiF4 相比 MXFP4 达到相近或更好精度时，所需“额外操作”更少（HiF4 只需 RHT 即可恢复精度；MXFP4 需要 RHT+SR+Truncation-free scaling），因此整体 slowdown 更小，更接近 FP4 的理论收益。\n(4) 目标是让线性层（含 dense 与 MoE）的大部分 GEMM 直接在 FP4 上执行，把辅助操作尽量限制在少量高精度阶段，从而实现端到端约 90% FP4 覆盖率。","experiments":"实验覆盖多模型家族与规模：Dense 模型包括 OpenPangu-1B 与 Llama3-8B；MoE 模型包括 Qwen3-MoE-30B。对比 HiF4 与 MXFP4 的预训练表现，以相对全精度 baseline 的 loss gap 衡量：HiF4 可做到约 ~1.0% 相对损失差距，MXFP4 约 ~1.5%。同时报告在稳定训练前提下，约 90% 的存储与计算在 FP4 中完成。论文还从“FP4 稳定化流水线的额外算子/高精度开销”角度分析不同方案的实际效率影响，指出某些恢复精度技巧会抵消部分 FP4 的吞吐优势。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读建议）\n1) Introduction：抓住 FP4 训练的主要失败模式（outlier→block scaling→下溢/偏置）以及为何需要 SR/RHT；这是理解后续设计取舍的前提。\n2) HiF4 格式描述：重点理解三层缩放各自的位宽/作用、64 元素 block 的选择，以及它如何同时改善动态范围与精度；建议把 HiF4 与 MXFP4 的缩放粒度与可表示范围做对照笔记。\n3) Low-Precision FP4 Training 流水线：逐步标注哪些算子在 FP4、哪些在 FP16/FP32，尤其是 RHT/SR/（MXFP4 的）truncation-free scaling 插入的位置与代价。\n4) 关键结果表/图：优先看不同模型（1B/8B/30B MoE）上的 loss gap 对比，以及“90% FP4 覆盖率”的统计口径（按 FLOPs、按 kernel 次数、还是按时间）。\n5) 工程与硬件相关段落：Ascend NPU 的矩阵单元/向量单元如何支撑 FP4 GEMM，哪些限制导致必须保留高精度步骤；这决定可迁移性。\n\nskim（泛读建议）\n- 先读 Abstract + Introduction 前半，建立问题：FP4 的梯度偏置与 outlier。\n- 跳到 HiF4 vs MXFP4 的核心结论段与主结果表：记住 HiF4 ~1.0% vs MXFP4 ~1.5% loss gap、以及 HiF4 需要更少稳定化技巧。\n- 快速浏览训练流水线图/伪代码（若有）以了解 RHT/SR 放在哪里即可。","authors_note":"作者强调这是面向能效 NPU（Ascend）的大规模 FP4 预训练系统性研究：HiF4 通过分层缩放在数值上更“抗 outlier”，因此在大模型与 MoE 上能以更少的稳定化辅助手段达到更小 loss gap；并展示在保持训练稳定的情况下可让约 90% 计算/存储落在 Hu","Junsong Wang","Xin Wang","Hu Liu","Yu Cheng","Ziwei Yu","Hongliang Li","Mehdi Rahimifar","Lei Yan","Xuefei Wang","Zhuang Ma","Lei Liu","Hui Yu","Anandharaju Durai Raju","Hoang Le","Hei Yi Golestan"],"notable_authors":[],"tags":["fp4","low-precision-training","ascend-npu","efficient-pretraining","moe"],"links":{"arxiv":"https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08826","pdf":"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.08826","github":null,"project":null,"source_url":null}},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"LLM pre-training is bottlenecked by compute and memory bandwidth. FP4 can greatly improve throughput and efficiency, but extreme low precision often destabilizes optimization—especially gradient quantization bias under outliers, where block scaling is dominated by maxima and most values underflow to zero. This paper investigates whether Huawei Ascend NPUs can support large-scale end-to-end FP4 pre-training using the HiFloat4 (HiF4) format, and whether HiF4 can achieve smaller loss gaps than MXFP4 with fewer stabilization tricks and thus less end-to-end slowdown.","importance":"If ~90% of training storage and compute can run in FP4 while keeping the loss gap to full precision around ~1%–1.5%, training cost and energy can drop substantially, enabling larger models and datasets under strict power constraints. The paper’s emphasis on how many auxiliary high-precision operations are required is crucial: these operations can erode the real end-to-end gains of FP4, so a format that needs fewer of them is practically more valuable.","technical_approach":"The work designs and evaluates an FP4 training pipeline on Ascend NPUs and compares FP4 formats.\n(1) Numeric format: HiF4 uses three-level hierarchical scaling with 64-element blocks: a top-level E6M2 scaler, second/third-level E1 scalers, and FP4 values in S1P2 (≈E1M2). This aims to expand dynamic range while retaining mantissa precision to reduce quantization error and gradient bias.\n(2) Stabilization: stochastic rounding (SR) is used for gradient quantization to reduce bias; Random Hadamard Transform (RHT) is applied in the backward pass for weight-gradient computation to decorrelate and spread outliers.\n(3) Key comparison: HiF4 reportedly needs only RHT for accuracy recovery, while MXFP4 needs RHT + SR + truncation-free scaling, implying HiF4 can reach better accuracy with less auxiliary overhead.\n(4) System goal: execute most linear-layer GEMMs (dense and MoE) directly in FP4, limiting higher-precision steps to the minimum necessary, achieving ~90% FP4 coverage.","experiments":"Experiments span dense and MoE LLMs: OpenPangu-1B and Llama3-8B (dense), and Qwen3-MoE-30B (MoE). Using loss gap vs a full-precision baseline as the metric, HiF4 achieves about ~1.0% relative loss gap while MXFP4 is about ~1.5%. The paper reports stable training with roughly ~90% of storage and computation performed in FP4. It also analyzes the computational implications of stabilization pipelines, highlighting that extra high-precision operations can offset FP4’s theoretical speedups.","reading_guide":"$1b","authors_note":"The authors position this as the first systematic study of large-scale FP4 LLM pre-training targeting energy-efficient Ascend NPUs. They argue HiF4’s hierarchical scaling is more robust to outliers, enabling smaller loss gaps with fewer stabilization tricks than MXFP4, and demonstrate that ~90% of training compute/storage can be done in FP4 while maintaining stable optimization—bringing FP4 closer to real end-to-end efficiency gains rather than isolated GEMM speedups."},"reading_tier":"must_read","recommendation":{"zh":"真正有用的是它把 FP4 训练稳定性拆成“需要多少高精度护栏”这条账，能直接指导你评估端到端加速是否兑现；建议对照 MXFP4 的消融表逐项抄作业。","en":"The value is the accounting of how many high-precision “guardrails” FP4 really needs, which determines whether end-to-end speedups are real; copy their MXFP4 comparison/ablation checklist."}},{"id":"2604.09258","title":"Nexus: Same Pretraining Loss, Better Downstream Generalization via Common Minima","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-10T12:17:18+00:00","category_id":"llm_pretrain","cover_url":"/covers/2604_09258.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.LG"],"summary":{"core_problem":"论文研究一个“同样预训练损失但下游泛化不同”的几何本质问题：在多数据源预训练（K个source的加权平均loss）中，优化最终收敛到的参数，是仅仅最小化了总和损失（Sum-of-Minima 型：对每个source各自的最优点可能很远），还是落在各source最优解的“共同区域/交集附近”（Intersection-of-Minima 型：对每个source的最优点都几何接近）。作者提出：这种“任务最小值之间的几何接近度（closeness）”与下游泛化强相关，即使预训练loss完全相同，closeness更高的解也会显著更好地下游表现。","importance":"该问题直指当下LLM预训练的核心瓶颈：预训练占据95%+算力与数据，但“把预训练loss压到同一水平”并不保证下游能力一致。论文给出一个可操作的解释框架：下游差异来自优化隐式偏置（implicit bias）导致的“落点几何形态”不同，而不仅是目标函数值不同。若成立，则意味着在不增加算力/数据、甚至保持相同预训练loss的前提下，可以通过改变优化轨迹/偏置来换取显著下游收益（作者报告的收益量级相当于翻倍算力）。","technical_approach":"（must_read：详细技术分析）\n1) 几何假设与形式化：将预训练视为K个数据源loss的加权和。作者区分两类达到相同L_train的极小点：Sum型（只对总和最优）与Intersection型（同时接近每个L_k的最优点）。核心量是“closeness”：各任务最优点之间/与训练解之间的几何距离（论文将其作为二阶性质，强调与曲率/海森矩阵相关）。\n2) 理论动机（quadratic/i.i.d.）：在简化的二次损失且任务分布同分布的设定下，作者给出结论（文中提到Theorem 2.2）：在相同预训练loss下，Intersection型解在下游任务loss上严格优于Sum型解。直觉是：若各任务最优点更“对齐/接近”，则对新任务（同分布抽样）更可能接近其最优点。\n3) 可计算代理：直接优化closeness不可行，因为需要每步知道每个L_k的精确最优点。作者证明/论证“任务梯度相似度”CosSim(∇L_i, ∇L_j)可上界closeness：若训练过程中不同source的梯度方向始终一致，则它们的最优点必然一致（或高度重合），从而closeness高。\n4) Nexus算法：目标是在不改变预训练目标（仍最小化原始L_train）的同时，引入一种优化器级别的机制去“最大化跨任务梯度余弦相似度”。关键在于近似计算并利用∇CosSim(∇L_i,∇L_j)（涉及二阶信息/梯度的梯度），并将其与基础优化器（Adam/Muon等）结合，形成一种偏置：在更新方向上鼓励不同数据源的梯度更对齐，从而把收敛点推向Intersection型共同极小区域。\n5) 机制解释（与下游泛化的连接）：作者在实验部分（Sec.5.1）声称观察到：训练中提升的梯度相似度与几何closeness不仅在训练source之间成立，也能“泛化”到下游任务（即下游梯度与训练梯度更一致/更可迁移），从而在相同预训练loss下得到更低下游loss与更高指标。","experiments":"作者在多种设置验证“same pretraining loss, better downstream”：\n- 规模：130M到3B参数。\n- 数据：不同预训练数据与混合比例设置。\n- 优化与训练策略：不同学习率schedule、不同基础优化器（如Adam/Muon等）与不同训练算力预算。\n- 主要结论：几乎所有设置下，Nexus在保持预训练loss相同的前提下，使下游loss降低>0.02（作者强调该幅度通常需要约2×预训练算力才能获得）。\n- 代表性指标（3B）：GSM8K +15%，MATH500 +8%，HumanEval +4%（相对提升口径按论文表述）。","reading_guide":"（must_read：精读建议）\n1) Introduction + Fig.2：必须精读。Fig.2用“Sum vs Intersection”直观定义了论文要解决的几何差异，也是后续所有论证的语义锚点。\n2) “Closeness: A Second-Order Property Related to Generalization”章节：重点看closeness的数学定义、它为何被称为二阶性质、以及它与下游泛化的连接假设（这里决定了方法是否有说服力）。\n3) 理论部分（含Theorem 2.2及其假设）：建议逐条核对假设（quadratic、i.i.d.、同分布下游任务等）与结论边界，理解它提供的是“动机/方向性保证”还是“可迁移的严格保证”。\n4) Nexus方法细节：重点看如何近似/计算∇CosSim(∇L_i,∇L_j)，需要哪些额外计算（是否引入HVP、额外前后向、采样多少task对），以及与基础优化器如何耦合（是改梯度、改动量、还是加正则项）。\n5) Sec.5.1（机制验证）：必须看作者如何实证“梯度相似度/几何closeness能泛化到下游”。建议重点关注：度量定义、统计方式（跨层/跨步平均）、对照组（同loss对齐）、以及是否排除了“只是更好调参/更强正则”的替代解释。\n6) 结果表格：优先看“同预训练loss对齐”的对照（而非同step或同token），因为论文主张的关键是‘loss相同但下游不同’。\n（skim：泛读建议）\n- 只想抓主旨：读Introduction+Fig.2、方法概述段（Nexus=最大化跨source梯度余弦相似度的优化偏置）、以及主结果表（3B在GSM8K/MATH/HumanEval）。\n- 想判断是否可用：快速扫方法的计算开销描述与实现细节（是否需要多source并行梯度、是否显著增加吞吐成本）。","authors_note":"作者的核心立场是：在多源预训练中，决定下游泛化的不仅是“把平均loss降到多低”，还包括“落在什么样的共同极小几何结构里”。Nexus试图在不改变预训练目标值的情况下，通过提升跨数据源梯度对齐来诱导更‘共同’的解，从而获得可观下游收益；并强调这种收益量级可媲美显著增加预训练算力，体现优化隐式偏置的重要性。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Huanran Zhu"],"notable_authors":[],"tags":["pretraining","optimization","generalization","common-minima","multi-source-data"],"links":{"arxiv":"https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09258","pdf":"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.09258","github":null,"project":null,"source_url":null}},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"The paper asks a geometric question behind the phenomenon “same pretraining loss, different downstream generalization.” In multi-source pretraining (average of K source losses), does optimization converge to (i) a minimizer of the summed loss that can be far from each source’s own minimizer (Sum-of-Minima type), or (ii) a solution lying near the intersection/common region of per-source minima (Intersection-of-Minima type)? The authors hypothesize that the geometric closeness among task/source-specific minima is strongly correlated with downstream generalization: even at identical pretraining loss, Intersection-type solutions can yield much better downstream loss/performance.","importance":"This targets a central bottleneck in modern LLM training: pretraining consumes 95%+ of compute/data, yet matching pretraining loss does not guarantee matching downstream capability. The paper frames downstream gaps as arising from optimizer implicit bias that selects different geometric solutions at the same objective value. If correct, one can obtain sizable downstream gains without extra tokens/compute—potentially comparable to scaling compute—by steering optimization toward “common minima.”","technical_approach":"$1c","experiments":"The paper validates “same pretraining loss, better downstream” across:\n- Model scales: 130M to 3B.\n- Data: different pretraining corpora and mixtures.\n- Training setups: various LR schedules, base optimizers (e.g., Adam/Muon), and compute budgets.\nMain findings: in nearly all settings, Nexus reduces downstream loss by >0.02 versus base optimizers while matching pretraining loss (a gap the authors argue often requires ~2× pretraining compute). On the 3B model, reported gains include +15% GSM8K, +8% MATH500, and +4% HumanEval (as stated in the paper).","reading_guide":"$1d","authors_note":"The authors’ thesis is that downstream generalization depends not only on how low the averaged pretraining loss is, but also on which geometric solution (common vs merely aggregate) the optimizer implicitly selects. Nexus aims to bias optimization toward common minima by increasing cross-source gradient alignment, delivering substantial downstream gains without improving (or even changing) the final pretraining loss."},"reading_tier":"must_read","recommendation":{"zh":"它把“同 loss 不同下游”归因到多源最小值的几何 closeness，给了可操作动作：用优化/采样策略去追 common minima 而非继续压 loss；建议重点看定义、度量与控制实验可信度。","en":"Explains “same pretrain loss, experiments."}},{"id":"2604.09406","title":"OASIS: Online Activation Subspace Learning for Memory-Efficient Training","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-10T15:19:54+00:00","category_id":"llm_pretrain","cover_url":"/covers/2604_09406.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.LG"],"summary":{"core_problem":"论文解决LLM训练的“内存而非算力”瓶颈，尤其是激活（activations）在大batch/长序列下占据峰值显存的大头。现有低秩方法多压缩权重/梯度/优化器状态，但对激活要么需要改架构，要么用固定投影导致随训练分布漂移而失效。核心问题是：能否在不改变前向计算的前提下，在线追踪并更新一个低维激活子空间，把反向所需的激活以低秩形式存储，从而同时压缩激活、梯度与优化器状态，并保持训练效果？","importance":"激活显存随序列长度与batch线性增长，常成为大模型训练/微调的硬约束。若能在不牺牲精度、且不改前向结构的情况下把激活存储从O(Nd)降到O(Nr)，就能直接换取更长上下文、更大batch或更大模型；同时若梯度与优化器状态也被同一机制低秩化，可进一步降低总体显存，使训练更“可规模化”。论文还指出激活子空间在训练中持续漂移（Fig.1(b)），因此“在线更新”是关键而非锦上添花。","technical_approach":"（must_read：详细技术分析）\n1) 关键观察（线性层梯度在激活张成空间内）：对线性层，权重梯度可写为G_W = X^T G_out，因此G_W位于输入激活X的列空间/张成空间内。这意味着：若用一个rank-r正交基U_t近似表示激活X≈X U_t U_t^T，则梯度也可在同一子空间内得到最优rank-r近似。\n2) 激活压缩但前向精确：OASIS不改前向计算；只在“为反向存储的中间激活”上做投影压缩：\n- 存储：\\tilde X_t = X_t U_t（维度N×r），而不是X_t（N×d）。\n- 反向重构/使用：梯度计算在低秩空间进行，得到\\tilde G_t（r×m），再通过U_t投回全空间更新参数。\n3) 梯度与优化器状态的联动低秩化：由于梯度被表示为低秩（r×m），Adam等优化器的一阶/二阶矩也可在低秩空间维护（显存从O(dm)降到O(rm)）。更新时再乘U_t映射回全维。\n4) 在线子空间学习（核心创新）：子空间U_t不是固定的，因为激活分布随参数更新而漂移。作者用Oja’s rule做流式PCA式更新，避免频繁对激活统计做精确特征分解（eigendecomposition）。\n5) 投影感知的状态更新：当U_t变化时，低秩动量/方差等状态必须与新子空间对齐，否则会出现“状态在旧基底、梯度在新基底”的不一致导致不稳定。作者借鉴LDAdam的projection-aware更新：在子空间更新后，对已有低秩状态做相应的投影/旋转对齐，保证优化过程稳定。\n6) 复杂度与收益：每层把激活存储从Nd降到Nr；梯度与优化器状态从dm降到rm。额外开销来自维护U_t与投影运算，但目标是在显存显著下降的同时保持吞吐与精度可接受。","experiments":"实验覆盖微调与预训练：\n- 任务：GSM8K、HumanEval、C4等；模型为Llama系列不同规模。\n- 关键现象验证：激活子空间漂移在训练全程非零（Fig.1(b)），支持“必须在线更新”。\n- 主要结果：在保持竞争性精度下，OASIS峰值显存最高可降至全量微调的约1/2（2×更省）；相对LDAdam在相近精度下进一步节省30%+显存；在更激进压缩（更小r）时优于既有低秩方法。预训练场景也保持有效，说明不仅限于微调。","reading_guide":"（must_read：精读建议）\n1) Fig.1(a)(b)：先看清“显存构成”与“子空间漂移”两条证据链。Fig.1(b)是方法必要性的关键论据。\n2) Methodology：逐式推导线性层梯度G_W = X^T G_out为何保证“梯度在激活张成空间内”，以及rank-r投影后为何得到“最优rank-r梯度近似”。\n3) Algorithm 1（若有）：精读整体训练流程：何时收集激活统计、何时更新U_t、何时投影存储、反向如何用\\tilde X_t与U_t计算更新。\n4) Oja’s rule更新细节：重点看学习率/步长、正交化（re-orthonormalization）频率、数值稳定技巧，以及这些超参对漂移跟踪与训练稳定性的影响。\n5) Projection-aware optimizer state：这是工程成败点。建议重点看：U_t变化后动量/方差如何变换；若不做会出现什么退化；与LDAdam的差异。\n6) 消融实验：优先看固定子空间 vs 在线子空间、不同rank r、不同层是否共享r/是否分层设置，以及在长序列/大batch下的峰值显存曲线。\n（skim：泛读建议）\n- 只想抓主线：读Introduction（动机+贡献）、Methodology前半（投影压缩激活→梯度/状态低秩化）、以及主结果表（显存节省与精度对比）。\n- 想快速评估可落地性：扫实现细节（是否需要改算子/自定义CUDA、对吞吐影响、与FlashAttention/梯度检查点的兼容性）。","authors_note":"作者强调两点：第一，激活显存是训练规模化的主要瓶颈之一；第二，激活的主子空间在训练中持续漂移，固定投影会变“陈旧”并伤害优化。OASIS用在线子空间学习把激活压缩与低秩优化统一起来，在不改前向的前提下同时压缩激活、梯度和优化器状态，从而获得显著峰值显存收益并保持性能。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Sakshi Choudhary","Utkarsh Saxena","Kaushik Roy"],"notable_authors":[],"tags":["memory-efficient-training","activation-compression","low-rank-subspace","optimizer-state"],"links":{"arxiv":"https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09406","pdf":"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.09406","github":null,"project":null,"source_url":null}},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"The paper tackles the memory bottleneck in LLM training, focusing on activation memory which often dominates peak footprint for large batch sizes and long sequences. Prior low-rank methods mainly compress weights/gradients/optimizer states, while activation-focused approaches often require architectural changes or rely on fixed projections that become stale due to activation distribution drift. The core question: can we track an evolving low-dimensional activation subspace online and store backprop activations in that subspace—without changing forward computations—so that activations, gradients, and optimizer states are jointly compressed while preserving training quality?","importance":"Activation memory scales linearly with sequence length and batch size and frequently becomes the hard constraint in large-scale training/finetuning. Reducing stored activations from O(Nd) to O(Nr) can directly enable longer context, larger batches, or larger models. If gradients and optimizer states are also represented in the same low-rank structure, total memory drops further. The paper highlights that activation subspaces drift throughout training (Fig. 1(b)), making online adaptation essential rather than optional.","technical_approach":"$1e","experiments":"Evaluations cover finetuning and pretraining:\n- Tasks: GSM8K, HumanEval, C4; models: Llama family at multiple scales.\n- Evidence for necessity: activation subspace drift remains non-zero throughout training (Fig. 1(b)).\n- Main results: up to ~2× lower peak memory than full finetuning at competitive accuracy; >30% peak-memory reduction relative to LDAdam at comparable accuracy; better performance than prior low-rank methods under aggressive compression (small r). Gains persist in pretraining, indicating robustness across settings.","reading_guide":"$1f","authors_note":"The authors emphasize that (1) activation memory is a primary scaling bottleneck, and (2) activation principal subspaces drift continuously, so fixed projections become stale and harm optimization. OASIS unifies activation compression with low-rank optimization via online subspace learning, achieving large peak-memory savings while keeping the forward pass unchanged and maintaining performance."},"reading_tier":"must_read","recommendation":{"zh":"在线学习激活子空间来省显存这条路很对味，关键看它在分布漂移下是否稳定且实现复杂度可控；建议先读 Fig.1(b) 漂移证据和显存/吞吐-精度权衡表。","en":"Online activation-subspace tracking is the right Models","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-03-18T07:49:13+00:00","category_id":"llm_pretrain","cover_url":"/covers/2604_08564.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CL","cs.LG"],"summary":{"core_problem":"扩散式语言模型（dLLM）在推理时需要决定“先解哪些 token/按什么顺序解码（permutation / order）”。现有解码顺序多用基于 token 置信度/熵/边际的局部贪心规则，只利用输出分布的局部信息，忽略全局序列结构，且缺乏与“最大化目标序列对数似然”之间的明确理论对应，因此常产生次优解码轨迹与质量损失。","importance":"解码顺序是 dLLM 并行解码效率与生成质量的核心瓶颈：顺序选得好可以在更少迭代/更高并行度下达到更高似然与更好质量；顺序选得差则会把全局依赖“解错/解晚”，导致错误传播或需要更多迭代修正。该工作试图把“顺序选择”从经验启发式提升为可解释、可证明的近似最优策略，并给出训练无关（training-free）的可落地算法。","technical_approach":"（must_read 级别技术分析）\n1) 概率视角的目标：将“解码顺序选择”形式化为优化问题。论文对比两种似然：\n- 实用的 permutation-based factorization likelihood：按某个解码排列逐步预测未解 token；\n- permutation-independent likelihood：理想化地让每个 token 都在“已知其余所有 token”的条件下被预测（相当于全局条件化的上界/参照）。\n目标是最小化两者之间的 log-likelihood gap（或其上界），从而把顺序选择与似然最大化直接挂钩。\n\n2) 关键理论结论：在一层 Transformer（softmax self-attention）分析框架下，论文证明该 gap 的上界与注意力矩阵的结构相关，尤其与“注意力列和（column sum）”相关。直观上，某个 token 的列和大，表示它被许多位置强烈关注/对全局表示贡献大（或在信息流中更“中心”）。\n- 结论：按注意力矩阵列和从大到小解码，可近似最小化该上界，从而近似最大化目标序列的对数似然。\n这给出一个从 self-attention 结构到解码顺序最优性的“形式化桥梁”。\n\n3) 算法实例化：Attn-Sampler（training-free）。\n- 与现有 token-level sampler（confidence/entropy/margin）不同：Attn-Sampler 不在输出概率空间做局部贪心，而是直接利用 Transformer 的 attention matrix 来决定每一步最“信息关键”的 token 集合。\n- 可扩展性：提出 block attention approximation，避免显式计算完整注意力矩阵（与高效 attention kernel 兼容）。\n- 并行度控制：提出 dynamic attention thresholding，根据序列级依赖强弱自适应调节每步解码的 token 数（在质量与并行之间动态折中）。\n\n4) 与既有方法的理论对比：论文进一步从其理论框架解释为什么纯 token-level 指标可能偏离似然最大化目标：它们只看“当前 token 的不确定性”，但不刻画该 token 在全局依赖图中的结构重要性，因而容易在关键枢纽 token 上解码过晚或在局部高置信但全局不关键处浪费步数。","experiments":"论文报告在多个基准上 Attn-Sampler 相比现有 dLLM 解码策略在“准确性/质量”和“速度/并行解码效率”上均有稳定提升；同时通过 block-wise 近似与动态阈值实现可扩展推理。实验还包含对不同采样器的对比分析，用以验证“注意力结构驱动顺序”相对“输出分布局部贪心”的优势。（若你需要具体数据点/表格结论，我可以在你提供 PDF 或关键实验页后逐项抽取。）","reading_guide":"must_read（精读建议）\n- 重点章节：\n  1) Introduction：明确问题定义（order selection）与现有 token-level 贪心的不足。\n  2) 理论推导章节（提出 gap、上界、与 attention column sum 的关系）：这是论文核心贡献，建议逐步对照符号理解“permutation-based vs permutation-independent”两种似然及 gap 的定义。\n  3) Attn-Sampler 方法部分：关注“如何从 attention 得到排序/并行解码集合”、dynamic thresholding 的规则、以及 block attention approximation 的复杂度与实现细节。\n  4) Experiments：优先看与 confidence/entropy/margin 等 sampler 的对照表，以及速度-质量折中曲线。\n- 重点图表/要点：\n  - 证明主定理（attention 动态阈值）。\n\nskim（泛读建议）\n- 先读 Introduction + 方法总览（Attn-Sampler 流程图/伪代码）+ 主实验对比表。\n- 理论部分只抓结论：‘按 attention 列和从大到小解码 ≈ 更接近最大似然’，以及它为何比置信度/熵更“全局”。","authors_note":"作者的核心立场是：dLLM 的解码顺序不应仅由 token 的局部不确定性决定，而应由模型内部的全局依赖结构决定；self-attention 提供了可解释且可证明的结构信号。Attn-Sampler 试图以“理论可解释 + 训练无关 + 工程可扩展”的方式，把该信号转化为更优的并行解码策略。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Yuyan Zhou","Kai Syun Hou","Weiyu LLMs (dLLMs) must choose a decoding order/permutation: which tokens to unmask first during iterative denoising. Existing strategies are mostly token-level greedy heuristics (confidence-, entropy-, or margin-based), relying on local output statistics and ignoring global sequence structure. They also lack a clear theoretical link to maximizing the target sequence log-likelihood, often leading to suboptimal decoding trajectories and generation quality.","importance":"Decoding order is a central lever for both quality and efficiency in dLLMs: a good order can reach higher likelihood/quality with fewer iterations and higher parallelism, while a poor order delays globally important tokens and wastes steps. This work elevates order selection from ad-hoc heuristics to a theoretically grounded, approximately optimal strategy, and provides a training-free algorithm suitable for practical inference.","technical_approach":"$20","experiments":"Across multiple benchmarks, Attn-Sampler consistently improves both generation quality/accuracy and inference speed/parallel decoding efficiency compared to prior dLLM decoding strategies. Models","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-10T05:08:39+00:00","category_id":"llm_pretrain","cover_url":"/covers/2604_08964.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CL"],"summary":{"core_problem":"半自回归（Semi-AR）解码是 dLLM 中常用推理框架：把序列分成若干 block，按 block 依次完成解码。但该机制存在“block 边界约束”：必须先完成当前 block 才能开始下一个 block，导致大量其实早已稳定（与最终输出一致且后续保持不变）的跨 block token 被无谓延迟解码（Block-Boundary Delay），浪费迭代步数并抑制局部区域的收敛传播（radiative effects）。关键难点变成：如何可靠识别这些跨 block 稳定 token 并提前解锁？","importance":"Semi-AR 的 block 约束直接限制并行度与速度上限，同时还可能损害质量：稳定 token 的延迟会阻断其对邻域的“辐射式”稳定促进，拖慢整体收敛。若能在不引入训练成本的前提下，准确提前解锁跨 block 稳定 token，就能同时提升推理效率与生成质量，并可作为通用 plug-and-play 解码增强模块。","technical_approach":"（must_read 级别技术分析）\n1) 现象与三条关键洞察：\n(I) Naive lookahead 不可靠：即便 token 已达到稳定状态，后续步骤仍可能出现短暂波动；仅凭局部一步/少数步的置信度变化会误判。\n(II) 稳定性与“收敛趋势”强相关：跨 block 稳定 token 在首次稳定后，其置信度呈现快速上升的“绝对稳定趋势（absolute stability trend）”。因此应基于轨迹趋势而非单点阈值。\n(III) 历史信息在标准解码中被隔离：常规迭代解码每一步只依赖上一步，最终输出只取最后一步，早期轨迹信息未被用于稳定性判断。\n\n2) AHD：Anchor-based History-stable Decoding（训练无关、即插即用）。\n- 核心机制：在每个解码步，把“当前步”作为动态 anchor，并回溯历史缓冲区（historical buffer）中的若干先前步，检查候选 token 在一段历史窗口内的预测一致性/趋势一致性，从而构造基于历史一致性的稳定性判据。\n- 目标：尽早捕捉 absolute stability trend 的出现，避免等待置信度达到很高的静态阈值；同时对局部波动更鲁棒。\n- 结果：一旦判定为跨 block 稳定 token，即可打破 block 边界提前解锁/解码，从而“Breaking Block Boundaries”。\n\n3) 理论支撑：论文声称对该方法给出理论证明（核心应围绕：历史一致性判据能在一定条件下更早/更可靠地识别稳定 token，并降低误解锁风险）。精读时建议把证明与 Figure 2 的经验现象对应起来理解：为何趋势比峰值更关键、为何回溯窗口能过滤短暂波动。","experiments":"论文在语言、视觉-语言、音频-语言等多模态/多领域任务上评估，结论是 AHD 在性能（质量/准确性）与推理效率（更少步数/更高并行度或更低延迟）上均稳定优于先前解码策略，并显著缓解 Semi-AR 的 block 边界延迟问题。文中通过图 1/图 2 等可视化展示 cross-block stable token 的普遍性、辐射效应以及置信度轨迹特征。（如需逐任务指标，请提供 PDF 或实验表格页以便精确摘录。）","reading_guide":"must_read（精读建议）\n- 重点章节：\n  1) Introduction：务必结合 Figure 1 理解 Block-Boundary Delay 与 radiative effects 的动机。\n  2) 稳定性分析章节：重点看 Figure 2（naive lookahead 的失败案例、absolute stability trend 的定义与证据）。\n  3) AHD 方法细节：动态 anchor、历史缓冲区长度/回溯策略、稳定性判据的具体形式，以及如何与 Semi-AR 框架集成（何时解锁、解锁多少）。\n  4) 理论证明部分：把证明中的条件与实际解码轨迹现象对齐，理解其“早解锁且稳”的原因。\n  5) Experiments：优先看跨领域（language / VLM / audio-language）一致性，以及消融（没有历史/没有 anchor/不同窗口大小）。\n- 创新点核对清单：\n  1) 明确提出并系统刻画 Semi-AR 的 block 边界延迟与跨 block 稳定 token；\n  2) 用“趋势”重定义稳定性，并指出历史信息隔离是关键障碍；\n  3) AHD：动态 anchor + 历史回溯的一致性判据，训练无关、可插拔。\n\nskim（泛读建议）\n- 先看 Figure 1/2 + 方法伪代码/流程图 + 主实验表。\n- 理论证明可先跳过，只保留直觉：用历史轨迹识别稳定 token，避免局部波动误判，从而提前跨 block 解锁。","authors_note":"作者强调 Semi-AR 的主要瓶颈不是模型能力而是“解码调度（schedule）”受 block 约束；跨 block 稳定 token 的延迟既浪费步数又抑制局部收敛传播。AHD 的设计哲学是：稳定性应由历史轨迹趋势来定义，并通过打破历史信息隔离实现更早、更稳健的解锁；同时保持 training-free 与 plug-and-play 以便广泛适配现有 dLLM。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Shun Zou","Yong Wang","Zehui Chen","Lin Chen","Chongyang Tao","Feng Zhao","Xiangxiang (Semi-AR) decoding is widely used in dLLMs: the sequence is decoded block by block, and the next block cannot start until the current one finishes. This creates an inherent block constraint that delays many tokens which are already stable across blocks (they match the final output early and remain unchanged). The resulting Block-Boundary Delay wastes steps and can hurt quality by suppressing local convergence propagation (radiative effects). The key challenge is to reliably identify cross-block stable tokens and unlock them early.","importance":"The block constraint limits the achievable parallelism and latency of Semi-AR decoding, and can also degrade generation quality by delaying stabilizing signals that help neighboring tokens converge. A training-free, plug-and-play method that accurately unlocks cross-block stable tokens can improve both efficiency and quality, and can be broadly applied to existing dLLM inference pipelines.","technical_approach":"$22","experiments":"Experiments span language, vision-language, and audio-language domains. Figures (e.g., Fig. 1–2) visualize the prevalence of cross-block stable tokens, radiative effects, and characteristic confidence trajectories. (Provide the PDF to extract exact metrics per benchmark.)","reading_guide":"$23","authors_note":"The paper argues Semi-AR’s main bottleneck is decoding scheduling under block constraints rather than model capacity. compatible."},"reading_tier":"skim","recommendation":{"zh":"这是个干净的推理期小补丁：用 anchor 识别跨 block 已稳定 token 来打破半自回归边界；只需看稳定判据与速度/质量曲线，别深究叙述。","en":"A clean inference-time patch: anchors detect cross-block insufficient search (beam width, calibration size, per-layer epochs) nor lack of PV-tuning, but codebook initialization: standard greedy / residual k-means sequential initialization frequently lands Key empirical findings:\n- Regime-change evidence: at 2 bpp, greedy initialization can cause catastrophic perplexity, and increasing beam width only partially mitigates it.\n- Basin persistence: after end-to-end PV-tuning, OA-EM remains consistently better across configurations; large initial gaps can shrink dramatically yet OA-EM still wins.\n- Asymmetric scaling with search: increasing beam width can help OA-EM but may hurt the greedy baseline post-PV, suggesting extra search is mainly beneficial within a good basin.\n- Pareto dominance: OA-EM improves the quality–compute frontier, achieving lower perplexity and better downstream accuracy at matched compute budgets.","reading_guide":"$26","authors_note":"The authors’ main message is that extreme (2-bit) free-form additive quantization is often limited by a structural optimization issue—bad basins induced by greedy initialization—rather than by insufficient downstream compute. paper asks whether more training data is worth its cost, but studies it in a deliberately controlled tiny setting: an attention-only decoder where embeddings and the output projection are frozen and MLP sublayers are removed. The central question is whether dataset-size scaling in this component-isolated Transformer still shows smooth improvements with clear diminishing returns (scaling-law-like behavior), and how much data is needed to approach full-data performance.","importance":"Most scaling-law studies operate at industrial scale and often co-scale model size, data, and compute, making causal attribution difficult. For compute- and data-constrained pretraining or prototyping, knowing when additional data yields diminishing returns is directly actionable. By constraining learning largely to self-attention parameters, this work provides a more interpretable testbed for isolating dataset-size effects under fixed capacity, and yields a practical “fraction of data for most of the performance” rule of thumb in this setting.","technical_approach":"$27","experiments":"Under a fixed attention-only architecture, the authors train across multiple dataset subset sizes and report validation token-level accuracy. 与 active 参数预算相关的项（类似 dense 网络，只是把总参数替换为 active 参数）；\n  - MoE 特有的“路由组合开销”项（来自路由模式数量的对数因子/额外复杂度）。\n  直观上：MoE 的统计复杂度 =（每次实际用到的网络容量）+（你允许模型在样本间切换多少种子网络/专家组合）。\n3）在内在维度 d 的数据模型下做 ERM 泛化：采用 d 维 C^1 流形上的数据分布假设，目标函数属于 C^β(ℳ)。将上面的覆盖数界代入标准平方损失 ERM 的 uniform generalization 分析，得到“逼近误差 + 估计误差 + 路由开销”的三部分分解；其中逼近/估计的主导指数由内在维度 d 而非环境维度 D 决定。\n4）构造性逼近定理：证明存在 MoE 架构在给定 active 参数预算下可达到经典的 C^β 在 d 维流形上的最小极大逼近速率，指数为 −2β/d（文中强调这是经典 minimax 指数）。这一步把“MoE 只要按 active 参数计量，就能恢复 dense 网络的逼近缩放”形式化。\n5）缩放律结论：当以 active parameter budget 为横轴时，MoE 可恢复 dense 网络在 (d,β) 控制下的模型/数据/计算最优缩放指数；最坏情形下路由只额外引入对数级（log）开销。作者也明确指出：如果实证更好，通常来自数据依赖的路由稳定性/专家专门化等非最坏情形效应。","experiments":"该论文主线为理论工作（覆盖数、逼近与泛化界、缩放律推导）。在给定的全文片段中未呈现系统实验部分；作者将结论定位为“保守的统计基线”，并强调与真实训练动力学/数据依赖路由行为可能存在差距。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读建议）\n- 先读 Introduction：抓住三件事——active capacity vs routing combinatorics 的分离、内在维度 d 的动机、以及“保守基线”定位。\n- 精读 MoE Model and Approximation Theory：\n  1）Definition 3.1（MoE Transformer 类与 top-k 路由设定）；\n  2）active attention+expert budget 的定义（这是后续所有缩放律的“横轴”）；\n  3）Theorem 3.2（构造性逼近，指数 −2β/d，常数依赖关系）。\n- 重点追踪“覆盖数分解”的证明结构：条件化固定路由 → 得到与 active 参数相关的 covering → 对路由模式 union bound → 路由开销项出现（通常是 log 级）。\n- 泛化界部分建议对照三项分解：逼近项（由 β,d 与 active 参数决定）+ 估计项（由 n 与复杂度决定）+ 路由项（组合数/对数项）。\nskim（泛读建议）\n- 只看：Introduction（贡献列表）+ 逼近定理主结论（−2β/d）+ 泛化/缩放律的最终形式（强调“按 active 参数计量恢复 dense 指数，路由带 log 开销”）。\n- 证明细节可跳过：覆盖数推导与 union bound 的技术细节只需理解其来源与为何是“额外对数项”。","authors_note":"作者反复强调该理论是 worst-case 的 uniform generalization 基线：它能“认证”哪些缩放行为不依赖优化与数据依赖效应；若实践中 MoE 表现更优，往往需要用路由稳定性、专家专门化、结构偏置等更细的、非最坏情形分析来解释。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Mansour Zoubeirou a Mayaki"],"notable_authors":[],"tags":["mixture-of-experts","scaling-laws","generalization-bound","routing","theory"],"links":{"arxiv":"https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09175","pdf":"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.09175","github":null,"project":null,"source_url":null}},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"MoE Transformers introduce conditional computation: only a small subset of experts is active per token. The theoretical gap is how to separate (a) benefits driven by per-input active capacity from (b) statistical overhead induced by the combinatorics of routing patterns. Dense scaling laws based on total parameters mischaracterize MoE, while counting only active parameters ignores routing multiplicity.","importance":"The paper provides a conservative, optimization-agnostic statistical baseline for MoE: a clean decomposition of complexity/generalization into an active-parameter term plus a routing-combinatorial term. f(X)) 联系起来，进一步用平方多重相关系数 ρ_l^2 与非高斯性指标 κ_l 给出非高斯情形的界（Theorem 4.4）。整体上是把 Roberts(2022) 的 GP/核近似思路扩展到有限宽网络的、可操作的层级近似框架。\n7）计算复杂度：证明总计算开销相对 MHA 为 (4/3)(1-4^{-L})，上界 4/3，与层级数 L 无关地被常数控制（Proposition 4.9），解释其实用性。","experiments":"在 ListOps（T=512）与 sequential CIFAR-10（T=1024）上，相比重训的 MHA baseline，分别提升约 +4.7pp 与 +1.98pp；计算开销约 1.31×。并对层级数 L∈{1,2,3,4} 与 stride s∈{2,3} 做敏感性分析，显示收益对超参较稳健。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读建议）\n- Section 3（Architecture + Kernel theory）：\n  1）HKT 的层级下采样、每层注意力、上采样融合的完整定义；\n  2）Proposition 3.6（频带/尺度解释）把“为什么多尺度有效”讲清楚；\n  3）Proposition 3.1/3.4（PSD 条件与 Gram 分解、秩界）理解其核化结构与容量控制；\n  4）Proposition 3.7（包含性）确认表达力不弱。\n- Section 3.6（Asymmetric score analysis）：重点看对称-反对称分解及其语义（reciprocity vs directionality），这是理解“理论 PSD 条件 vs 实际训练模型”差异的关键。\n- Section 4（Approximation theory）：精读 Theorem 4.4 与三项误差分解，理解互信息/相关性/非高斯性如何决定逐层级收益。\n- Section 5（Experiments）：重点看与 MHA 的对比设置、计算开销对齐方式、以及 L、s 的敏感性图表。\n\nskim（泛读建议）\n- 只看：Introduction（动机与贡献）+ Section 3 的架构图/公式（弄清多尺度如何做）+ Proposition 4.9（复杂度常数上界）+ 实验主表（ListOps/CIFAR-10 提升与 1.31× 开销）。\n- 理论细节可略读：核 PSD 条件与信息论界的推导过程；保留结论与变量含义（I、ρ^2、κ）即可。","authors_note":"作者强调他们不是通过稀疏化注意力矩阵来“省算力”，而是通过跨尺度分解来引入结构先验；同时也坦承训练后的实际注意力打分往往不满足 PSD 条件，因此专门给出非对称打分的分解分析来解释其可用性。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Giansalvo Cirrincione"],"notable_authors":[],"tags":["efficient-attention","multi-scale-attention","kernel-transformer","theory","long-context"],"links":{"arxiv":"https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08829","pdf":"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.08829","github":null,"project":null,"source_url":null}},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"Standard self-attention is scale-blind: it allocates the same architectural capacity to all token pairs regardless of distance, which hurts tasks requiring simultaneous short- and long-range reasoning and incurs quadratic cost in sequence length. The paper asks when image tokens become representationally stable/redundant, whether deeper image-token computation is functionally interchangeable, how this depends on task type (single-token prediction vs multi-token generation), and whether fine-tuning or structured reasoning can recover performance after truncating image-token processing.","importance":"Answering this determines whether a large fraction of VLM compute is avoidable. Safeguarding Multimodal LLMs","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-10T01:01:56+00:00","category_id":"multimodal","cover_url":"/covers/2604_08846.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.LG","cs.AI","cs.CL","cs.CV"],"summary":{"core_problem":"多模态大模型（MLLM）在面对文本 jailbreak 与图像对抗（如排版触发、反事实语义、不可感知扰动）时容易输出有害/违规内容。现有安全方案（提示词、响应过滤、微调）分别存在脆弱、需要重复调用、或成本高的问题。激活（表示）steering 虽然灵活，但现有方法要么概念集合太小、要么强度难校准、要么 SAE 特征缺乏语义落地导致难以精确控制某个安全概念而不伤及其他能力。论文要解决的是：在冻结模型参数的前提下，实现“可扩展、可标注、可精细解耦”的多概念安全控制。","importance":"DACO 把“概念词典（可解释、可扩展）”与“稀疏自编码器 SAE（可组合、可控）”结合，试图同时解决覆盖面、可控性与可解释性三难：用大规模概念库支撑更丰富的激活基底学习，并把 SAE 原子自动对齐到词典概念与安全标签，从而在推理时以较低开销对冻结 MLLM 做细粒度安全 steering，且尽量保持通用效用。这类方法对快速应对新型攻击模式、跨模型迁移（QwenVL/LLaVA/InternVL）具有现实意义。","technical_approach":"（must_read 级别：详细技术分析）\nDACO 的核心是“词典对齐的稀疏分解 + 可标注的 SAE 原子 + 推理时系数级干预”。\n1) 大规模概念词典构建（§3.1）：\n- 从 WordNet 抽取 >15,000 个概念；\n- 从 CC-3M 检索约 400,000 个 caption-image 对构建 DACO-400K；\n- 将这些样本喂给目标 MLLM，收集指定层/位置的激活，并按概念聚合得到 concept vectors（概念向量）；\n- 将概念划分为 desirable/undesirable（与安全任务相关的“应增强/应抑制”概念集合）。\n关键点：相比以往 <20 个 steering 向量的做法，DACO 用数量级更大的概念覆盖来刻画激活空间几何结构，并为后续稀疏建模提供“字典”。\n2) 基于词典的稀疏编码与概念移除（§3.2）：\n- 将某层残差流激活表示为少量概念向量的线性组合（稀疏分解）；\n- 通过抑制/移除 undesirable 概念对应的系数，实现对有害概念的定向压制；\n- 该路径强调“训练开销低/可训练-free 或轻量”的控制，并提供一定语义可解释性（系数对应概念）。\n3) 词典初始化与自动标注的 SAE（§3.3）：\n- 训练 SAE 以学习更“表达力强”的稀疏基底（atoms），用于更好地覆盖激活空间；\n- 用概念词典来初始化 SAE decoder（让 atoms 从一开始就贴近可解释概念方向，而不是纯数据驱动的不可名状特征）；\n- 通过“最近邻概念向量”把 SAE atoms 自动注入语义标签与安全标签（undesirable/desirable），降低人工探针与解释成本。\n4) 推理时 steering 机制：\n- 在选定层对稀疏系数做干预：增强 desirable atoms 的系数、抑制 undesirable atoms 的系数；\n- 目标是在不改参数的情况下提升安全性，同时尽量保持通用能力。\n5) 相对现有方法的差异化：\n- 相比对比提示得到的 steering vectors：DACO 覆盖更广、冗余更少，并通过稀疏性提升可组合控制；\n- 相比纯 SAE：DACO 通过词典对齐解决“特征无语义锚点”的痛点，并支持自动标注与更可控的概念级调节；\n- 相比过滤/微调：推理时一次前向即可干预，无需 rerun 或昂贵训练。","experiments":"论文声称在多个基准（如 MM-SafetyBench、JailBreakV）与多个代表性 MLLM（QwenVL、LLaVA、InternVL）上验证：显著提升安全性，同时保持通用效用。精读时建议重点核对：\n- 安全指标：攻击成功率/违规率下降幅度，是否覆盖文本+图像攻击类型；\n- 效用保持：通用 VQA/对话基准是否掉点，掉点与 steering 强度的关系曲线；\n- 可控性：是否展示“只抑制某类概念不影响其他概念”的解耦实验（概念干预的选择性/正交性）；\n- 规模效应：概念数量（15k）与样本量（400k）对效果的边际收益；\n- 消融：无词典初始化的 SAE、无 SAE 仅词典稀疏编码、不同层/不同干预位置的对比；\n- 运行开销：推理时额外计算（稀疏编码/SAE 前向）与延迟。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读建议）\n- Figure 1/3（框架与流水线）：先把“词典→概念向量→稀疏分解→SAE 对齐→推理干预”的数据流与张量流走通。\n- §3.1：概念抽取、DACO-400K 构建、激活聚合方式（在哪一层、如何池化、如何去噪/去歧义）决定词典质量。\n- §3.2：稀疏编码目标函数、稀疏度约束、以及 undesirable 概念移除的具体算子（投影/截断/缩放）与强度标定。\n- §3.3：SAE 结构、decoder 初始化细节、atoms 自动标注（最近邻度量、阈值、冲突处理）是“可解释+可控”的关键。\n- §4：跨模型与跨基准泛化；重点看安全-效用 trade-off 曲线与消融表。\n\nskim（泛读建议）\n- 读 Introduction 把握三大痛点（概念少、强度难调、SAE 无语义）。\n- 快速扫 §3：理解 DACO 的三步（大词典、稀疏分解、词典对齐 SAE）。\n- 直接看 §4 主结果表与消融，确认是否“安全显著提升且效用基本不掉”。","authors_note":"作者把 MLLM 安全 steering 的关键瓶颈归因于“概念覆盖不足”和“稀疏特征缺少语义锚点”。DACO 用大规模词典为激活空间提供可解释坐标系，并用词典初始化与自动标注把 SAE 的控制能力转化为可操作的安全概念旋钮，从而在冻结模型下实现更可扩展、更细粒度的安全控制。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Jinqi Luo","Jinyu Yang","Tal Neiman","Lei Fan","Bing Yin","Son Tran","Mubarak Shah","René LLMs can be induced to produce harmful/policy-violating outputs via text jailbreaks and image-based adversarial inputs (typographic triggers, counterfactual semantics, imperceptible perturbations). Prompting, response filtering, and finetuning are respectively brittle, require reruns/extra compute, or are expensive. Activation steering is flexible but existing MLLM steering often covers too few concepts, is hard to calibrate, and SAE features lack semantic grounding—making it difficult to adjust one safety concept without collateral damage. The goal is scalable, semantically grounded, fine-grained safety control on frozen MLLMs at inference time.","importance":"DACO combines a curated concept dictionary (interpretable and scalable) with sparse autoencoders (compositional and controllable) to address coverage, controllability, and interpretability simultaneously. 动态重权，强化与视觉证据强相关的生成片段；同时对后期步骤施加更强的视觉补偿以缓解遗忘。\n- Inter-trajectory（轨迹间）：在候选响应组内，整体优先“视觉累积更好/更持续 grounding”的轨迹，使策略更新倾向于长期保持视觉对齐的解答路径。\n整体特点：不引入额外训练 Instructional Videos","starred":false,"priority":"p3","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-09T20:51:13+00:00","category_id":"multimodal","cover_url":"/covers/2604_08762.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CV","cs.AI"],"summary":{"core_problem":"现有视频-语言基础模型在教学视频（长、非裁剪、包含多步程序）中对“动作/动词语义”的理解不足：训练时容易被 ASR 文本噪声与弱对齐误导；表征上存在“静态偏置”（更依赖物体/背景等静态线索而非运动线索）；同时缺乏对多动作时序结构（步骤顺序、跨步对齐）的建模能力。","importance":"教学视频理解的关键不只是识别单一动作，而是识别细粒度动作并建模其时序组织（procedures）。若模型持续依赖名词/物体线索，将在动作检索、步骤定位、程序理解、可解释对齐等任务上出现系统性失真。该工作把“动作中心（action-centric）”从裁剪视频场景推进到真实网络教学视频场景，核心价值在于：在弱监督+多动作+噪声文本的现实设定下，提供可落地的动作表征预训练范式与诊断基准。","technical_approach":"InstrAction 是“数据侧强动作监督 + 模型侧去静态偏置 + 目标函数侧多动作对齐”的组合框架。\n1) 数据侧（LLM 辅助策展）：(a) 过滤非教学/不可视觉落地的字幕片段（对 ASR 噪声做二分类清洗）；(b) 从保留字幕中抽取结构化 verb phrases（如 V+N、V-ing、V+Prep+N）作为细粒度动作监督与时序锚点；(c) 构造动作中心 Hard Negatives：i) verb-altered HN（改动动词、尽量保持名词/物体不变）迫使模型区分“同物体不同动作”；ii) order-swapped HN（交换步骤顺序）迫使模型学习程序时序合理性。\n2) 模型侧（Action Perceiver 去冗余、聚焦运动）：在视频编码器产生的密集/冗余时空特征上，引入 Perceiver-style resampler 将其压缩为少量 latent action tokens，目标是提取“动作相关”而非“物体相关”的信息。\n3) Verb-guided distillation（动词引导蒸馏）：用 verb phrase embedding 对视频特征做注意力汇聚得到 teacher action tokens；Perceiver 输出的 latent tokens 作为 student，通过蒸馏约束把 latent 空间拉向动词语义/动作线索。推理时不依赖 verb phrase（只在训练时提供引导）。\n4) 目标函数侧（超越全局对比）：(a) DTW-Align：用 Dynamic Time Warping 在“视觉 action tokens 序列”和“文本 verb phrases 序列”之间做非线性对齐，适配教学视频中语速变化、描述跳跃、弱对齐等现象；(b) MAM（Masked Action Modeling）：在文本中 mask 动作 token/短语，让模型结合视觉证据与上下文预测，被设计为在噪声 ASR 下强化跨模态动作落地与融合。\n整体训练以对比学习为主干（视频-文本对齐），并通过上述数据/结构/辅助任务共同抑制静态偏置、增强动作可分性与时序理解。","experiments":"论文主张包含两类验证：\n(1) 预训练数据与诊断：在 HowTo100M 的 cooking video-language foundation models struggle with verb/action understanding in instructional videos (long, untrimmed, multi-step procedures). The main causes are (i) noisy, weakly-aligned ASR transcripts that provide unreliable supervision, (ii) a pervasive “static bias” where models over-rely on objects/backgrounds (and nouns) instead of motion cues, and (iii) insufficient modeling of multi-action temporal/procedural structure (step order and cross-modal alignment over time).","importance":"Instructional video understanding requires fine-grained action recognition plus temporal organization into coherent procedures, not just object-centric matching. Long-Term Agent Memory Compression for Efficient Streaming Video Understanding","starred":false,"priority":"p3","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-10T06:11:34+00:00","category_id":"multimodal","cover_url":"/covers/2604_09000.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CV"],"summary":{"core_problem":"流式视频理解中的“Agent记忆图”(以文本节点为主)会随时间快速膨胀，导致存储成本与检索延迟显著上升；在实时问答场景下，检索变慢会直接破坏可用性。同时，直接压缩记忆又容易丢失长期一致性与关键细节，造成准确率下降。","importance":"该工作瞄准“工业级超长流式视频”落地瓶颈：不是再优化KV cache或视觉token，而是压缩以明文组织的长期记忆图，使得在保持实体一致性与信息完整性的前提下，显著降低检索开销并提升实时性。","technical_approach":"提出训练-free 的 StreamMeCo：按记忆图连通性将文本节点分两类并分别压缩。\n(1) must_read：双分支压缩\n- 孤立文本节点(不指向face/voice实体)：用 Edge-free Minmax Sampling (EMsampling)。先对文本embedding聚类；每个簇内先选最靠近簇中心的代表点，再迭代执行“min-max/farthest point”策略：对每个未选点计算其到已选集合的最小距离，选择该最小距离最大的点加入，直到满足保留预算。直觉是用覆盖/多样性最大化保留语义跨度，避免只保留密集区域。\n- 连通文本节点(与face/voice相连、含实体指代)：用 Edge-aware Weighting Pruning (EWpruning)。先基于文本-实体(脸/声)边权构造权重矩阵，估计每个文本节点的“实体重要性”；再结合文本节点间embedding相似度，偏向选择更不相似(更去冗余)的节点；最终用融合分数决定保留集合，从而在保实体相关信息的同时减少重复描述。\n(2) must_read：检索阶段补偿\n- Time-decay Memory Retrieval (TMR)：将文本按时间分段，对每段计算该段文本与query的总相似度，据此动态分配每段可检索的节点配额；再对不同时间段施加非线性时间衰减，使近期段更“易被取回”，在压缩后仍能兼顾长期记忆与近期关键信息，缓解压缩带来的性能退化。\n(3) skim：整体流程\n先对记忆图做结构感知压缩(孤立/连通分治)，再用带时间衰减与动态配额的检索策略进行问答时的记忆召回。","experiments":"在三个高难度基准上评估(文中提到 M3-Bench-robo 等)。在约70%记忆图压缩条件下，实现约1.87×检索加速，同时平均准确率提升约1.0%(相对原检索/压缩基线)。并展示随文本节点数增长时，检索延迟快速上升的现象(用于证明压缩必要性)。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读建议）\n- 重点看：Introduction 中对“记忆图规模→检索延迟”的问题刻画与贡献点；Preliminaries 对 M3-Agent 记忆图结构与两类检索(字符/语义)的描述，这是理解“为何按连通性分治压缩”的关键。\n- 重点模块：EMsampling 的“聚类+farthest point”选择逻辑；EWpruning 的“边权(实体重要性)+embedding去冗余+融合打分”；TMR 的“按时间段总相似度分配预算+非线性衰减”两步。\n- 建议精读图表：Figure 1(节点数与检索延迟趋势)、Figure 2(记忆图结构与检索流程)。\n- 创新点抓手：结构感知(孤立/连通)的双分支压缩 + 检索端时间衰减补偿，且全流程训练free、可插拔到图记忆Agent。\n\nskim（泛读建议）\n- 先读：Introduction 的问题与方法概览；Preliminaries 的记忆图与检索机制；再快速扫“方法三件套”(EMsampling/EWpruning/TMR)的输入输出与直觉。\n- 结果只需看：在~70%压缩下的加速比与准确率变化，以及是否对不同数据集一致有效。","authors_note":"作者将“长期流式理解”的瓶颈从模型上下文转移到“可检索的外部记忆图”，并强调工业可用性：训练free、结构感知压缩、检索端补偿。核心立场是：压缩不应一刀切，而应利用图连通性区分实体相关与非实体信息，并在检索时用时间机制恢复鲁棒性。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Junxi sink影响)；直接基于相似度的聚类会产生空间碎片化簇，池化后对象几何结构被破坏，导致表征失真。","importance":"该工作系统性“复盘并推进”两类主流剪枝信号(显著性attention与多样性similarity)，给出可插拔的改造：既提升显著token选择对多模态/长尾的覆盖，又让聚类合并更符合视频对象的时空局部性，从而在极低保留率下保持性能并显著加速。","technical_approach":"提出 Tango 框架，包含三模块：时间分段、显著token选择、时空合并。\n(1) must_read：显著token选择的改造\n- 观察：attention热图常呈多模态(对应不同语义实体)，且分数长尾；硬Top-k会偏向单一峰值或被固定位置的attention sink占据，导致语义覆盖不足。\n- 方法：引入“diversity-driven”选择：先扩展候选集合，再对候选token做聚类，并在簇内进行选择(而非全局Top-k)，以覆盖多个注意力模式与尾部信息，实现更全面的语义保留。\n(2) must_read：相似度聚类的局部性注入\n- 问题：仅用特征相似度聚类会把同一对象切成碎片簇，池化后形状结构丢失。\n- 方法：在相似度计算中加入时空局部性先验，惩罚时空距离远的token被判为相似；具体通过 Spatio-temporal Rotary Position Embedding (ST-RoPE) 编码空间与时间相对距离，使相似度对“近邻一致、远邻区分”更敏感，并可无缝接入标准聚类/合并流程。\n(3) skim：整体流程\n先做时间分段以最大化可剪的静态token；再用多样性驱动的显著选择保留关键token；最后用带ST-RoPE的相似度进行时空合并/池化，得到更干净的对象级表示。","experiments":"在 Video LLM 上进行综合实验。报告在仅保留10%视频token时，LLaVA-OneVision-7B可保持约98.9%的全量性能，同时推理加速约1.88×。并通过可视化/统计展示注意力多模态与长尾分布、以及直接聚类导致的碎片化现象，用以支撑方法设计动机。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读建议）\n- 重点看：Introduction LLM inference is dominated by the LLM’s Transformer cost, which scales with the number of visual tokens. Existing training-free pruning has two major issues: (1) rigid attention Top-k selection fails under multi-modal, long-tailed attention distributions and can be hijacked by attention sinks; (2) plain similarity-based clustering often yields spatially fragmented clusters, and pooling over them distorts object representations by breaking geometric structure.","importance":"The paper advances the two mainstream pruning paradigms (attention-based saliency and similarity-based diversity) with plug-and-play fixes: better coverage of attention modes/tails during selection and locality-aware similarity for cleaner object-level merging—enabling strong accuracy retention at very low token budgets with notable speedups.","technical_approach":"$3b","experiments":"Comprehensive experiments on Video LLMs show that keeping only 10% of video tokens preserves ~98.9% of full performance on LLaVA-OneVision-7B while achieving ~1.88× inference speedup.
