decide."}},{"id":"2604.08579","title":"On the Spectral Geometry of Cross-Modal Representations: A Functional Map Diagnostic for Multimodal Alignment","starred":false,"priority":"p3","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-03-28T04:20:54+00:00","category_id":"multimodal","cover_url":"/covers/2604_08579.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.LG","cs.AI"],"summary":{"core_problem":"论文研究“独立预训练”的视觉编码器（DINOv2）与文本编码器（MiniLM）在不联合训练、仅靠少量配对锚点（anchors）的情况下，能否通过一种具有几何可解释性的方式实现跨模态对齐；并进一步诊断两种模态表征流形在“内在复杂度”和“谱基方向/取向”上是否一致。","importance":"主流跨模态对齐（如 CLIP）依赖海量配对数据与端到端联合训练，模块化差：新增模态往往要重训。若能对“独立预训练”表征做后对齐，将显著降低多模态系统扩展成本。本文的价值不在于提出更强检索方法（结果为负），而在于提供一套谱几何诊断工具，揭示独立预训练模型之间“复杂度相近但取向不一致”的结构性鸿沟，为 Platonic Representation Hypothesis 提供了不同于 CKA 的证据维度。","technical_approach":"核心方法是将跨模态对齐表述为 functional map（功能映射）：把两个表征空间各自视为由样本点构成的离散流形，在各自 embedding 上构建 kNN 图（k=15），用高斯核权重并以第 k 近邻均值距离设带宽 σ，得到对称加权图；计算归一化图拉普拉斯 L=D^{-1/2}(D-W)D^{-1/2}，做特征分解得到低频谱基（前 k 个特征向量）作为“内在坐标系”。\n对齐被表示为谱基之间的紧致线性算子 C∈R^{k×k}，通过带正则的最小二乘求解：一方面拟合锚点对应（paired anchors）在谱域的系数映射，另一方面加入拉普拉斯可交换性（commutativity）惩罚，鼓励 C L_v ≈ L_t C（在 functional map 文献中对应近似等距/同胚条件下的结构保持）。\n论文强调 functional map 相比在“环境空间”直接做线性对齐（Procrustes/CCA）具有三点理论吸引力：可组合性（A→C 可由 A→B 与 B→C 相乘得到）、低频截断带来的谱正则、以及在近似等距假设下的可分析误差界。\n但作者也指出：独立预训练的视觉/语言表征很可能不满足近似等距（isometry）假设，从而 functional map 的“对齐能力”可能受限；因此本文更侧重把它当作诊断工具而非强基线。","experiments":"数据与设置：在 Flickr30k 上抽取 N 个图文样本，分别用 DINOv2 与 all-MiniLM-L6-v2 编码；在各自 embedding 上构图、求谱基；用不同数量锚点监督学习对齐。\n对比方法：functional map（本文）、Procrustes、CCA、relative representations，以及联合训练范式代表 CLIP（作为参考上界）。\n主要结果（负结果）：跨模态检索上 functional map 全监督预算下均显著落后。示例：100 个锚点时 i2t Recall@1 仅 2.2%，而 Procrustes 12.1%，relative representations 13.4%，且锚点更多时差距扩大。\n谱几何发现（正洞见）：两编码器的拉普拉斯特征值谱非常接近（normalized spectral distance=0.043），表明两者“内在复杂度/频谱结构”相似；但 functional map 矩阵 C 几乎没有对角占优（diagonal dominance<0.05），且正交性误差很大（orthogonality error=70.15），同时存在明显的拉普拉斯可交换性违背。按 functional map 理论语义：对角占优≈共享谱取向，近正交≈近似等距；两者都不成立。\n结论：提出“spectral complexity–orientation gap”——独立预训练模型可能在捕获结构的“复杂度”上趋同，但在该结构的“谱基取向/坐标系”上并不对齐，这解释了为何 functional map（依赖结构保持/近等距）难以直接带来强检索性能。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读：详细技术分析 + 建议）\n1) Introduction：重点读作者为何引入 functional map（可组合性/谱正则/误差界）以及为何“负结果更有科学价值”。\n2) Methodology §3.1-§3.2：精读 kNN 图构建（权重、σ 设定、对称化）、归一化图拉普拉斯定义、谱基截断的含义；以及 functional map 的优化目标（锚点拟合项 + commutativity 正则）与求解细节。\n3) Diagnostics §3.4（或对应章节）：这是本文最可复用的贡献。务必弄清三个量：diagonal dominance、orthogonality error、Laplacian commutativity violation 的定义、直觉与在 functional map 文献中的几何语义。\n4) 实验结果部分：重点对照“检索失败”与“谱诊断成功”的并置叙事，理解作者如何从 C 的非对角/非正交推导出 isometry 假设失效。\n5) 关键图表建议：\n- 两模态拉普拉斯特征值谱对比图（支撑 spectral distance=0.043）。\n- functional map 矩阵 C 的可视化（看是否对角占优/块结构）。\n- 诊断指标随锚点数变化的曲线（看监督增加是否改善取向）。\n创新点抓手：把 functional map 从形状匹配迁移到“神经表征流形对齐”；提出谱复杂度相似但取向不一致的 gap；给出可量化诊断指标体系。\n\nskim（泛读：方法概述 + 建议）\n- 先读 Introduction 的问题设定与结论段：functional map 不提升检索，但揭示谱结构现象。\n- 快速扫 Methodology：知道流程=编码→kNN 图→图拉普拉斯谱分解→解 C（带 commutativity 正则）。\n- 直接看结果与诊断：记住两个数字结论（spectral distance 0.043；diagonal dominance<0.05/orthogonality error 70.15）以及“complexity–orientation gap”的解释。\n- 若只关心工程检索：看与 Procrustes/relative representations 的对比表即可。","authors_note":"作者明确将本文定位为“诚实的负结果 + 有信息量的诊断”：functional map 在跨模态检索上不如简单线性对齐与相对表征，但它揭示了独立预训练视觉/语言表征在谱复杂度上高度相似、在谱取向上显著不一致的结构性事实；并据此认为 functional map 依赖的近似等距假设对该场景不成立。"},"metadata":{"institutions":["Indian Institute of Technology Generation","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv","huggingface"],"published_at":"2026-04-10T09:53:27+00:00","category_id":"multimodal_gen","cover_url":"/covers/2604_09168.png","hf_upvotes":11,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CV"],"summary":{"core_problem":"论文关注视觉生成模型在“高质量”与“参数/内存效率”之间的矛盾：传统做法通过堆叠大量不共享参数的 Transformer 层来提升容量，导致参数量与显存占用线性增长、吞吐受“memory wall”限制。作者提出能否用循环/权重共享的 Transformer，在保持生成质量的同时显著减少参数，并且让模型在推理时可按算力预算随时提前退出（Any-Time/Elastic inference）。","importance":"在图像/视频生成（Masked Generative Transformers、Diffusion Transformers）中，推理计算往往可以通过迭代步数扩展，但训练与模型参数仍昂贵。若能用“循环共享参数”把更多 FLOPs/迭代深度压到更少参数里，可带来：更低部署成本（端侧/多档位服务）、更高吞吐（减少跨层参数搬运）、以及数据受限时更强正则化。本文的关键在于解决 looped/recurrent transformer 的训练难点：中间循环的表示往往不可用，导致无法弹性退出。","technical_approach":"提出 Elastic Looped Transformers (ELT)：用少量 Transformer block 作为“循环体”，在前向中重复 L 次（loops），以迭代精炼的方式完成生成（可用于 MaskGIT 类并行迭代解码，也可用于 Diffusion Transformer 的多步去噪）。与深堆叠的非共享层不同，ELT 在循环间共享权重，从而显著降低参数量。\n训练关键是 Intra-Loop Self Distillation (ILSD)：在一次训练 step 内构造 teacher/student 双路径——teacher 运行最大循环数（完整 compute），student 选择 teacher 轨迹的子序列（更少 loops、提前退出点），并让 student 的中间输出/预测去拟合 teacher 的对应目标，从而把“后期循环才学会的复杂变换”压缩到更早循环，使得任意中间 loop 都能产生可用的高质量结果。由于 student 是 teacher 前向的子集且共享同一套参数，ILSD 不引入额外参数开销，训练开销也被设计为尽量可控。\n整体上，ELT 把‘深度’从“层数”改为“循环次数”这一可调计算旋钮：训练一次得到一族模型（不同 loop 数即不同 compute/quality 点），推理时按预算选择退出。","experiments":"论文报告在图像与视频生成上的参数效率与质量：\n- 类条件 ImageNet 256×256：FID 达到 2.0，并宣称相对 MaskGIT 等基线在参数量上约 4× 减少，同时在等推理计算（iso-inference-compute）下匹配或更优。\n- 类条件 UCF-101 视频生成：FVD 72.8，并相对 MAGVIT 等基线实现约 4× 参数减少。\n- Any-Time 推理：展示随着 loop 数增加，质量-计算形成可遍历的 Pareto 前沿；少 loops 适合低延迟/端侧，多 loops 适合高保真云端。\n- 可扩展性：作者强调该“循环计算旋钮”可迁移到 Masked Generative Transformers 与 Diffusion Transformers 两类框架，且随模型规模与 loop 数呈可预测缩放。\n（注：基于给定全文摘录，具体消融项/损失细节/训练配方与更多定量表格未完全展开，但核心结论围绕 ILSD 使中间 loops 可用、以及参数效率提升。）","reading_guide":"must_read（精读：详细技术分析 + 建议）\n1) Introduction：精读为何 looped 分布），以及如何保证“无额外参数、低额外开销”。\n3) 与两类生成范式的结合：\n- MaskGIT/Mask-based iterative decoding：关注循环与“逐步解 mask / 置信度排序采样”的接口。\n- Diffusion：关注循环与时间步/噪声预测器的关系（循环是替代更深网络、还是与扩散步数叠加）。\n4) Any-Time 结果图：重点看不同 loop 的质量曲线是否平滑、是否存在早退崩溃，以及 ILSD 是否显著改善中间 loop。\n5) 参数-计算对比表：核对“4× 参数减少”是在同等质量还是同等推理计算下成立。\n创新点抓手：权重共享循环 Transformer 用于高保真视觉生成；ILSD 让中间循环可用，从而一次训练得到可弹性推理的一族模型。\n\nskim（泛读：方法概述 + 建议）\n- 读 Introduction + 曲线/示例图。","authors_note":"作者的核心立场是：循环/权重共享能把“更多计算”装进“更少参数”，但必须通过 ILSD 让每个中间 loop 都具备可用生成能力，才能真正实现弹性推理与部署分层；并宣称在图像与视频生成上以显著更少参数达到强质量指标。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Sahil Goyal","Swayam paper targets the tension in visual generation between high synthesis quality and parameter/memory efficiency. Standard approaches scale by stacking many unique Transformer layers, increasing parameters and exacerbating the memory-wall bottleneck. The goal is to use recurrent, weight-shared Transformers to drastically cut parameters while keeping quality—and to enable Any-Time (elastic) inference by exiting after a variable number of loops.","importance":"For image/video generation (masked iterative decoders and diffusion transformers), compute can often be traded for quality via iterative refinement, but model parameters and memory footprint remain costly. A looped, weight-shared design can deliver more FLOPs per parameter, improve throughput by reducing parameter movement, and potentially regularize better in data-limited regimes. The key obstacle is training: intermediate loop states are often unusable until the final loop, preventing elastic early-exit. This paper’s contribution is a training strategy that makes intermediate loops meaningful.","technical_approach":"$3f","experiments":"Reported results emphasize parameter efficiency and Any-Time behavior:\n- Class-conditional ImageNet 256×256: FID 2.0, with a claimed ~4× parameter reduction vs MaskGIT while matching or improving under iso-inference-compute.\n- Class-conditional UCF-101 video generation: FVD 72.8, with a claimed ~4× parameter reduction vs MAGVIT.\n- Any-Time inference: qualitative/quantitative evidence that quality improves smoothly with more loops, enabling deployment tiers from low-latency few-loop inference to high-fidelity many-loop inference.\n- Scalability claim: the looping compute lever applies to both masked generative transformers and diffusion transformers with predictable scaling.\n(Note: based on the provided full-content excerpt, fine-grained ablations and full training recipe details are not fully visible, but the central experimental narrative is parameter-efficiency + elastic inference enabled by ILSD.)","reading_guide":"$40","authors_note":"The authors’ central claim is that recurrence/weight sharing can pack substantially more compute into far fewer parameters, but only becomes practically valuable for deployment if intermediate loops are high-quality. Generation for Diffusion Model Training","starred":false,"priority":"p3","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-10T06:36:38+00:00","category_id":"multimodal_gen","cover_url":"/covers/2604_09022.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CV"],"summary":{"core_problem":"扩散模型训练高度依赖大规模图文对数据，但纯扩散生成的合成数据常出现几何/语义不一致，并可能在“用生成数据再训练生成模型”的闭环中触发模型自噬（MAD）导致性能退化。论文要解决的是：如何可扩展地产生高一致性、高可用的合成图文对，用于扩散模型训练/补充真实数据，同时降低MAD风险。","importance":"数据是扩散模型能力上限的关键瓶颈：真实数据采集与标注昂贵且受隐私/安全/偏见约束；而扩散自生成数据虽便宜但会引入系统性伪影并放大分布偏差，甚至导致MAD。用3D场景+物理渲染生成数据能提供几何与光照一致性、可控元数据与可追溯来源，是构建“可规模化且更可靠”的训练数据的重要路线。BlendFusion的价值在于把3D渲染数据生产做成一条可自动化、可过滤、可去重的端到端管线，并证明关键设计（以物体为中心的相机采样）能显著提高可用样本产出率。","technical_approach":"方法是一条基于Blender/BlenderProc与路径追踪（path tracing）的合成图文对生成管线（BlendFusion），核心环节包括：\n1) 物体中心相机放置（object-centric camera placement）：对场景中每个mesh对象，取其AABB中心；在水平环上按方位角每45°采样8个视角（仰角固定0°近似“自然眼平视角”）；相机始终look-at对象中心。为保证构图一致与尺度稳定，依据对象在视线垂直平面上的投影高度来反算相机距离，使对象在图像中占据固定填充比例f（文中取2/3），从而不同大小对象都能获得近似一致的主体占比与可解释 framing。\n2) 渲染：使用Blender路径追踪输出物理一致的图像（几何/光照/材质一致性优于扩散直出）。\n3) 质量过滤：用启发式规则与视觉语言模型（VLM）过滤剔除“视觉次品”（如遮挡严重、构图失败、异常渲染等），提升训练可用性。\n4) 多样性采样/去重：过滤后再做相似样本消除与多样性保持的采样，避免同一对象/视角的冗余堆积。\n5) 自动标注：对保留图像进行自动caption生成，形成最终图文对。\n产物：用该管线构建FineBLEND数据集（7,500对图文），并用对齐度与美学指标与常用图文数据集对比分析，同时评估“物体中心相机策略”相对随机/全局采样的可用渲染产出提升。","experiments":"实验围绕三类问题展开：\n1) 数据集构建与统计：从多样3D环境渲染并过滤得到FineBLEND（7,500图文对）。\n2) 质量评估：使用图文对齐指标与美学指标对FineBLEND进行分析，并与若干常用图文数据集做对比（强调对齐与视觉质量）。\n3) 消融/对比：验证物体中心相机放置相对物体无关（object-agnostic）的相机采样能提高“可用渲染”的yield（减少遮挡/主体缺失/构图失败导致的废片）。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读建议：详细技术分析路径）：\n- 重点章节：\n  - Introduction：把问题钉在MAD与扩散合成数据伪影上，理解为何选择3D+物理渲染。\n  - BlendFusion方法段：逐行看“object-centric camera placement”的几何定义、8方位角采样、仰角固定、look-at、以及用投影尺寸反推相机距离以实现固定fill fraction（这是yield提升的关键机制）。\n  - Filtering与diversity sampling相关段：理解启发式+VLM过滤的判据类型，以及去重/多样性采样如何避免数据集被单一场景/对象主导。\n  - Dataset/Analysis/Experiments段：关注对齐度与美学指标的选择、与公开数据集对比的结论，以及yield提升的量化结果。\n- 重点图表：\n  - Figure 2（端到端pipeline图）：用于建立全局心智模型（资产→相机采样→渲染→过滤→去重→caption）。\n  - 相机放置示意/公式所在图表（若有）：用于复现相机距离计算与构图约束。\n- 创新点抓手：\n  1) 以对象为中心的系统化相机采样+尺度归一化构图；\n  2) 过滤（启发式+VLM）与多样性采样组合成“可规模化数据清洗”；\n  3) Introduction：抓住核心因果链：独立耦合→轨迹交叉→向量场学均值→曲率大→采样慢；以及κ-FC与MixFlow分别解决“对齐”与“可用性/权衡”的角色分工。\n  - Background（Rectified Flow + 轨迹交叉分析）：精读v*(xt,t)=E[x1-x0|xt]这一最优解形式，理解为何交叉会导致条件期望变成“平均方向”。\n  - κ-FC方法段：重点看其如何形式化“条件化源分布/耦合”，以及正则项与prior hole问题的讨论（这是MixFlow动机）。\n  - MixFlow训练策略：精读“线性混合源分布”的定义、训练/采样时的差异、以及为何能把结构从条件源迁移到高斯源；同时关注测试期可调的机制。\n  - 实验与消融：优先看步数-质量曲线、不同κ信息量对结果的影响、以及与SOTA轨迹拉直方法的公平对比设置。\n- 重点图表（建议优先级）：\n  - 展示轨迹曲率/交叉与采样步数关系的示意图；\n  - MixFlow的源分布混合示意与速度-质量可调曲线；\n  - 主表（FID vs steps）与消融表。\n- 创新点抓手：\n  1) κ-FC把“可学习耦合”推广到任意引导信号；\n  2) MixFlow用混合源分布解决耦合学习的正则权衡，并把折中从训练期移到测试期；\n  3) 以“减少轨迹交叉”作为统一解释框架连接理论与经验结果。\n\nskim（泛读建议：快速掌握要点）：\n- 读Introduction前两段+贡献列表，记住：问题是源-目标独立导致曲率；解法是κ-FC与MixFlow。\n- 读Background里对“交叉→学均值→变弯”的解释（不必推导细节）。\n- 直接跳实验主结果（FID提升百分比、所需步数减少情况）与一两个关键消融（κ是否信息化、混合比例影响）。","authors_note":"作者强调：采样慢并非只靠更强网络或更好ODE求解器就能解决，源分布与数据分布的耦合结构会决定轨迹是否交叉、是否弯曲；通过引入信息化的条件信号κ并用混合源分布把结构迁移到无条件源上，可以在更少步数下获得更好质量，并把速度-质量控制权交给测试阶段。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Nazir Nayal","Christopher Wewer","Jan Eric Lenssen"],"notable_authors":[],"tags":["rectified-flow","diffusion","source-distribution","sampling-efficiency","flow-matching"],"links":{"arxiv":"https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09181","pdf":"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.09181","github":null,"project":null,"source_url":null}},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"Rectified Flows / Flow Matching aim to straighten generative trajectories to reduce sampling steps, yet in practice they still require many function evaluations. A key cause of high curvature is the independence (misalignment) between the source distribution (typically standard Gaussian) and the data distribution, which induces many intersecting forward paths; the learned vector field then averages directions, producing curved trajectories and slow sampling. The paper tackles how to better align the source–target coupling / source distribution to reduce path curvature and achieve high quality with fewer steps.","importance":"Sampling speed is a primary deployment bottleneck for diffusion/flow-based generators. Rectified Flow is faster than diffusion but still not fast enough. Reducing steps without sacrificing quality/diversity directly lowers inference cost and enables more interactive generation. The paper’s significance is in reframing speed as a coupling/alignment problem and proposing (i) a general learnable coupling conditioned on arbitrary signals and (ii) a simple mixed-source training strategy that avoids brittle training-time hyperparameter trade-offs while enabling test-time speed–quality control.","technical_approach":"$43","experiments":"On standard image generation benchmarks, the paper reports:\n- ~12% FID improvement over standard Rectified Flow at a comparable number of sampling steps.\n- ~7% FID improvement over the strongest prior trajectory-straightening method under comparable steps.\n- Extensive analyses/ablations on how κ informativeness and design choices affect the learned source distribution, generation quality, and required sampling steps, including demonstrations of test-time controllable speed–quality trade-offs when κ is sufficiently informative.","reading_guide":"$44","authors_note":"The authors argue that slow sampling is fundamentally tied to source–data coupling structure, not just model capacity or ODE solvers. By conditioning couplings on informative signals κ and using a mixed source distribution to transfer structure to the unconditional Gaussian, MixFlow achieves better quality with fewer steps and enables test-time control of the speed–quality trade-off."},"reading_tier":"skim","recommendation":{"zh":"skim：把RF的弯曲归因到源分布不对齐是个会改变直觉的点；建议复现混合源分布对步数-质量曲线的影响，重点看不同κ下是否稳。","en":"Skim: attributing RF Maximum Principle in Optimal Control","starred":false,"priority":"p3","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-03-28T13:01:01+00:00","category_id":"multimodal_gen","cover_url":"/covers/2604_08580.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["math.OC","cs.LG"],"summary":{"core_problem":"扩散/流模型的“奖励微调（reward fine-tuning）”与从Boltzmann/tilted分布采样可统一表述为随机最优控制（Stochastic Optimal Control, SOC）问题：在SDE约束下学习最优控制以最小化代价/最大化回报。近期Adjoint Matching（AM）方法把该问题转成回归式损失并在实践中有效，但原工作主要是启发式、局限于控制仿射+二次代价等特殊设定，缺乏从控制理论一阶条件出发的严格推导，也难以推广到更一般的控制依赖漂移/扩散与更一般代价。本文要解决：为AM建立严格的SMP（随机最大值原理）理论基础，给出可推广的Hamiltonian形式目标，并解释其为何对应有效的“控制改进”步骤。","importance":"把生成模型后训练（对齐奖励、采样能量模型/玻尔兹曼分布）放到SOC框架下是近年的统一视角，但SOC的经典HJB/SMP求解在高维不可行。若AM能被严格证明为与SOC目标具有相同一阶变分、其临界点满足SMP/HJB驻点条件，并且梯度下降对应可解释的控制改进（MSA），则它将成为可扩展、可实现、可泛化的后训练算法基座：既能指导扩散/flow模型的reward fine-tuning，也能用于科学计算中的Boltzmann采样。","technical_approach":"must_read（详细技术分析）\n1）SOC建模：把“学习生成动力学以匹配tilted/Boltzmann分布”写成在SDE约束下最小化期望总代价（含running cost与terminal cost）的控制问题，控制可参数化为神经网络并影响漂移与/或扩散。\n2）从SMP推导AM：作者以随机最大值原理为起点，引入Hamiltonian与伴随（adjoint）过程，构造Hamiltonian视角的Basic Adjoint Matching（BAM）目标（Theorem 1）。关键结论：BAM目标的期望与原SOC目标具有相同的一阶变分（first variation），因此其临界点满足SMP/HJB的驻点条件。\n3）一般化：BAM覆盖“控制依赖漂移与扩散、凸running cost”等更一般设定；为实现无偏估计，需要一阶与二阶伴随方程来估计cost-to-go的梯度与Hessian。\n4）Lean AM（Theorem 2）：当扩散仅随时间变化（不依赖控制/状态）时，可化简为只需一阶项的lean AM损失，避免二阶伴随/二阶项，且在控制仿射+二次代价时退化回原始Adjoint Matching。\n5）优化动力学解释（Theorem 4）：作者进一步证明期望lean AM损失的梯度流等价于SMP导出的连续时间MSA（method of successive approximations）控制改进过程，并绕开经典SMP数值法中难处理的鞅（martingale）项；这为“用梯度下降优化AM损失”提供了原则性保证：每一步都是有效的控制改进。\n\nskim（方法概述）\n- 把reward fine-tuning/Boltzmann采样写成SOC；用SMP构造一个可训练的Hamiltonian adjoint matching损失（一般情形BAM，常用情形lean AM）；证明该损失与原SOC目标一阶等价、临界点满足最优性条件，并解释其梯度下降等价于SMP的控制改进迭代（MSA）。","experiments":"本文偏理论与方法论：核心“实验”是理论定理与推导（Theorem 1/2/4）给出的等价性、临界点性质与梯度流解释。应用层面主要对接既有工作（如对文本到图像flow matching的reward fine-tuning）与Boltzmann采样场景，强调可实现性与推广性；具体实证细节需重点查看论文后半的算法实现与（若有）实验段落/附录设置。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读建议：重点章节/图表/创新点）\n- Section 2：SOC表述与原始Adjoint Matching回顾（理解“原方法为何像回归”以及其局限）。\n- Section 3 + Theorem 1：Hamiltonian BAM的定义、伴随方程、以及“与原SOC目标同一阶变分”的证明主线（这是全文理论核心）。\n- Theorem 2：扩散仅随时间变化时的化简条件与lean AM损失形式（这是最可能直接用于生成模型后训练的版本）。\n- Theorem 4：梯度流=MSA的解释，尤其是如何绕开martingale项（这是把“可优化的损失”与“控制改进算法”连接起来的关键创新点）。\n- 实现细节/附录：无偏估计器、伴随ODE/SDE数值求解、以及在神经网络参数化下的可训练性假设。\n\nskim（泛读建议：推荐看哪些部分）\n- Introduction（问题统一视角与贡献列表）+ Section 2（SOC与原AM）+ Theorem 2（lean AM最终可用形式）+ Theorem 4（为何梯度下降有控制改进含义）。若只想落地，用lean AM相关算法段与实现细节即可。","authors_note":"作者的主张是：Adjoint Matching并非启发式技巧，而是可由SMP严格推出的Hamiltonian匹配目标；在常见“时间依赖扩散”设定下可得到无需二阶项的lean损失；并且优化该损失的梯度流等价于SMP的MSA改进过程，从而为生成模型reward fine-tuning of diffusion/flow models and sampling from tilted (Boltzmann) distributions can be formulated as stochastic optimal control (SOC) under SDE constraints. Adjoint Matching (AM) recently provided an effective regression-style objective, but it was originally heuristic and limited to special cases (e.g., control-affine dynamics with quadratic costs), lacking a rigorous derivation and generalization. This paper aims to place AM on firm theoretical ground via the Stochastic Maximum Principle (SMP), generalize it to broader SOC settings, and explain why optimizing the AM loss corresponds to principled control improvement.","importance":"SOC provides a unifying lens for post-training generative dynamics (alignment to rewards, energy-based/Boltzmann sampling), but classical HJB/SMP solvers are intractable in high dimensions. delta learning：不是绝对质量而是 chosen 与 rejected 的质量差（delta）驱动学习，并进一步追问：delta 的来源（生成器层面 vs 样本层面）分别起什么作用？样本层面的哪些推理维度差异最关键？结果是否依赖最终答案正确性？","importance":"这直接影响偏好数据构造与筛选策略：如果提升主要来自某些过程性质量维度（如步骤连贯性）而非结果正确性，那么可以用更便宜的生成器、更少的数据、甚至不依赖 outcome verification 来获得可观增益；同时也解释了为何“弱模型对的差异”能提升强学生，并为可验证推理（数学/STEM/代码）场景的对齐数据工程提供可操作的选择准则。","technical_approach":"提出并形式化两类 delta： (1) generator-level delta：chosen 与 rejected 由不同能力的生成模型产生，其能力差即 delta（数据构造层面的设计变量）。(2) sample-level delta：同一对样本内部的质量差，沿可解释推理维度度量。论文用校准的 LLM-as-a-judge 将每条 CoT 轨迹分解评估为五个维度：factuality、strategy coherence、step coherence、computational precision、signal-to-noise ratio，并据此计算 chosen-rejected 的维度差异；通过控制生成器配对与对样本按“高 delta”维度筛选，分析哪些维度的差异最能带来下游泛化增益。同时系统检验“正确性是否主导信号”：构造四种正确性组合（C/I、C/C、I/I、I/C）分别做 DPO，对比其对域内与域外任务的影响。","experiments":"三段式实验： (1) 迁移与尺度：在可验证推理任务上复现 delta learning，并用两大家族生成器（Nemotron-4B–49B、s1-3B–32B）构造偏好对；发现用 s1-7B vs s1-3B 的弱模型对、且不做 ground-truth verification，也能达到与“用 DeepSeek-R1 且带 outcome verification 的 DPO”相当的效果。进一步增大 generator-level delta（chosen 生成器更强）时：域内数学提升基本不随之变化，但域外 STEM/代码稳步提升。作者将其归因于 sample-level delta 随 chosen 变强而在五个维度上整体拉大，从而驱动域外增益。 (2) 正确性消融：在四种正确性配对上训练，发现域内表现对正确性标签基本不敏感，甚至 I/C（rejected 正确、chosen 错误）也能带来超过基座的增益，否定“结果正确性是主信号”。 (3) 维度分解与数据选择：按五个维度分别挑选 sample-level delta 最大的子集，发现 step coherence 是最稳定有效的选择准则；仅用约 5k 高-delta 样本即可匹配或超过全量 16.5k 的效果，说明精筛可替代扩大数据或扩大生成器差距。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读）：(1) Introduction + “Decomposing the judge 标定方式、按维度筛选的对照结果，以及 step coherence 为何最稳健。 (5) 数据效率结论：5k 高-delta≈16.5k 全量的实验设置与统计显著性。skim（泛读）：先读 Introduction + 两类 delta 定义；再快速看三条主结论图表：generator-level 扩展的域内/域外曲线、正确性四组合对比、以及按维度筛选（step coherence coherence）做高-delta 筛选，以更少数据获得相当或更好收益。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Chia-Hsuan Lee","Mingyang Zhou","Renkun Ni","Zelei Cheng","Sihui Dai","Supriyo Chakraborty","Shixiong Zhang","Sambit optimization (e.g., DPO/KTO) is widely used to align reasoning models, but it is unclear what signal in preference pairs actually drives downstream reasoning gains. Building on the delta learning hypothesis, the paper asks which notion of “delta” matters—capability gaps between generators vs within-pair quality gaps—and which specific reasoning-quality dimensions in the chosen/rejected traces are responsible. It also tests whether final-answer correctness is the dominant driver.","importance":"This directly informs how to construct and filter preference data for verifiable reasoning (math/STEM/code). If improvements come mainly from process-level quality differences (e.g., step coherence) rather than outcome correctness, then one can use cheaper generators, fewer pairs, and even avoid outcome verification while still improving strong students—turning alignment into a more data-efficient, mechanism-driven pipeline.","technical_approach":"The paper formalizes two deltas: (1) Generator-level delta: the capability gap between the models producing chosen vs rejected responses (a data-construction knob). (2) Sample-level delta: the within-pair quality difference measured along interpretable reasoning dimensions. Using a calibrated LLM-as-a-judge, each chain-of-thought trace is scored on five axes—factuality, strategy coherence, step coherence, computational precision, and signal-to-noise ratio—and deltas are computed per dimension. The authors then (a) vary generator pairings to study how generator-level delta translates into sample-level deltas and downstream gains, (b) construct preference pairs across four correctness combinations (C/I, C/C, I/I, I/C) to test whether correctness drives learning, and (c) select subsets with the largest sample-level deltas per dimension to identify which dimensions are most causally useful.","experiments":"$47","reading_guide":"must_read (deep): (1) Introduction + the delta definitions section to understand the generator→sample signal pathway. reasoning）”提升有限；根因在于缺少覆盖多种推理技能、且可自动验证的高质量训练数据。现有把 RLVR 扩展到更多“知识领域”的做法（如从网页抽取 QA）并不等价于提升通用推理技能，且验证困难、噪声大。","importance":"通用推理是现实任务与 BBEH/BBH 等基准的核心能力，但仅靠 STEM RLVR 甚至会出现“数学更强、通用推理更弱”的负迁移现象（文中举例 OpenReasoner/OpenThinker 在 AIME 大幅提升但 BBEH 下降）。因此，如何系统性构建“可验证 + 多技能覆盖 + 低成本”的 RLVR 数据，是把 RLVR 从 STEM 推向通用推理的关键瓶颈。","technical_approach":"提出 SuperNova：面向通用推理 RLVR 的数据策展框架，核心洞见是“高质量指令微调数据（如 SuperNI/FLAN）里包含专家标注的 ground-truth 与隐含推理模式”，可被系统改造为 RLVR 可验证样本。整体是多阶段 pipeline（论文图 2）：(1) 源任务筛选：从 SuperNI 候选任务出发，评估其对 BBEH 23 个子任务的推理能力迁移；并将部分开放式任务重格式化为可验证形式（例如改为多选）。结论：源任务选择对下游 pass@k 影响极大。(2) 任务混合策略：比较 macro mixing（全子任务共享一组平均最优任务）与 micro mixing（针对每个 BBEH 子任务分别选最优源任务）。结论：micro mixing 稳定优于 macro mixing，暗示不同推理技能需要不同“数据来源任务”来触发/训练。(3) 合成干预（数据增强）评估：尝试引入长上下文依赖等合成改写，但在固定训练预算下并未带来收益，说明“更复杂的合成扰动”不必然等价于更高 RLVR 数据质量。(4) 基于上述决策构建 SuperNova 数据集：约 25K 条 RLVR 样本，用于训练 Qwen3 0.6B–4B 等不同规模模型，并强调 test-time compute（多次尝试）带来的探索收益。","experiments":"作者进行了 100+ 次 compute-matched RL 实验系统比较数据设计决策。最终在 BBEH-test 上，SuperNova-4B 相对提升 pass@1 约 29.4%、pass@8 约 42.9%，并显示从 1 次到 8 次尝试性能显著上升（更好的推理探索）。值得注意的是，SuperNova-4B 在通用推理 pass@8 上超过更大的 Qwen3-8B 约 8.2%，体现“更小模型 + 更好数据/训练范式”可胜过更大基座。并在 BBH、MMLU-Pro、Zebralogic 等额外基准上表现出跨任务泛化提升（文中提到如相对提升 12.3% 等）。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读）：1) Introduction：重点看“STEM 提升不迁移甚至负迁移到 BBEH”的动机与问题定义（general reasoning 的边界）。2) Figure 2（pipeline 总览）：把每个阶段的输入/输出、可验证化改写、以及与 RLVR 训练闭环对应起来。3) §3.1（源任务选择与可验证化）：这是论文最关键的“数据为何有效”的证据来源，关注哪些 SuperNI 任务被证明能触发 BBEH 子技能，以及开放式→可验证的具体改写原则。4) mixing 实验（macro vs micro）：理解“按子技能定制数据配方”的结论与其对通用推理的含义。5) 合成干预无效的消融：关注作者如何控制训练预算、为何增强不增益（对后续复现/扩展很重要）。6) §6 主结果与 scaling（0.6B–4B、pass@1 vs pass@8）：理解 test-time compute 与训练数据之间的交互。\nskim（泛读）：1) 直接看 Figure 2 + 数据集规模（25K）与关键结论（micro mixing 更好、合成增强无效）。2) 看 BBEH 主表（pass@1/pass@8）与“4B 超 8B”的对比结论。3) 快速扫额外基准（BBH/MMLU-Pro/Zebralogic）确认泛化趋势。","authors_note":"作者的核心主张是：通用推理 RLVR Advantage","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-09T18:22:31+00:00","category_id":"post_train","cover_url":"/covers/2604_08690.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.LG","cs.CL"],"summary":{"core_problem":"在 RLVR 中，GRPO 这类“仅看最终结果(outcome-only)”的方法稳定有效，但理论上更强的“细粒度 dense reward/advantage（按推理步骤/token）”在实际采样预算下反而更差。论文指出关键原因：用 Monte Carlo（从中间前缀采样多条续写并用最终对错回传）估计早期 token 的 advantage 时方差极高且符号经常出错（sign-inconsistent），导致训练方向不稳定，最终不如直接把 outcome reward 广播给所有 token 的 GRPO。","importance":"这揭示了 RLVR 走向更细粒度信用分配（credit assignment）的结构性矛盾：细粒度信号上限更高，但在可承受的推理采样预算下难以可靠估计，导致“理论更好、实践更差”。解决该矛盾对提升推理过程质量、减少无效思维链、并在相同预算下获得更强性能至关重要。","technical_approach":"提出 SKPO（Skip-Connected Policy Optimization），把一次推理分解为 upstream（上游，早期推理段）与 downstream（下游，后续推理段）两阶段，并只在一个中间位置实例化 Monte Carlo 采样，从而在不爆炸采样成本的情况下给上游提供相对细粒度的学习信号。关键设计：1) Upstream：生成“早停”的推理片段 s，并用从该位置继续采样得到的 downstream 结果的 outcome reward 聚合成对 s 的 MC 奖励；上游采用 single-stream optimization 来降低细粒度信号的不稳定性（通过更低的每 prompt 样本需求、以及用历史样本估计更稳定 baseline）。2) Downstream：仍用 GRPO 式组内相对优势（group-relative）做 outcome 级优化，但引入 skip connection，把输入从仅 q 变为 [s, q]（将上游片段与原问题拼接），使模型既能利用有帮助的上游推理，又保留一定探索自由度。3) 工程优化：通过 single-pass rollout 让总体计算量与 GRPO 近似持平。论文还提出“implicit advantage”现象：即使最终对错相同，SKPO 训练出的轨迹中间步骤质量更高，这是由优化结构自发涌现而非额外监督。","experiments":"实验在数学推理基准上展示 SKPO 相对 GRPO 的显著提升，并强调在 OOD（分布外）上也更稳健。分析部分用图 1 等展示：在现实采样预算下，MC + group-relative 的早期 token advantage 高方差且频繁符号翻转，从而解释 dense reward 方案为何会稳定落后于 outcome-only GRPO。进一步分析显示 SKPO 产生更高的中间步骤质量（implicit advantage），说明其在“过程优化”上确实改善了信用分配。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读）：1) Figure 1：理解作者的核心反直觉发现（早期 token advantage 的高方差与 sign error）以及它如何直接导致 dense 方法不如 GRPO。2) Methodology/§3.1：重点看 token-level MC 奖励的形式化、为何 t 越靠后 MC 越收敛到 outcome（从而 GRPO 可视为极限情形），以及“只在单一中间点采样”的动机。3) Figure 2（算法框架）：把 upstream/downstream、single-stream、skip connection [s,q]、以及 single-pass rollout 的计算复用关系彻底读懂。4) §3.2（目标函数）：对照两阶段各自的 policy gradient 目标，理解为何上游不用 group-relative、下游保留 group-relative。5) 实验与消融：关注在相同采样/计算预算下与 GRPO 的对比，以及 implicit advantage 的度量方式（如何评估中间步骤质量）。\nskim（泛读）：1) 先看 Introduction + Figure 1 把问题抓住：dense MC 在早期不可靠。2) 看 Figure 2 + 方法小结把 SKPO 的两阶段与 [s,q] skip connection 记住。3) 快速看主结果表确认“同预算优于 GRPO + OOD 更稳”。","authors_note":"作者的关键贡献不是“发明更复杂的奖励模型”，而是指出 dense MC credit assignment 在有限采样下的统计失败模式（高方差+符号错），并用结构化两阶段优化把 MC 采样放到一个中间点：上游用更稳的单流优化吃细粒度信号，下游继续用 GRPO 的稳定相对优势；skip connection 让下游既继承上游优点又不被其锁死，从而在计算不增的前提下获得更好的过程质量与最终性能。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Fengwei Teng","Jinyi Bai","Xinhao Yao","Demi Ruohan Wang","Jiahao Zhao","Zhijiang Guo"],"notable_authors":[],"tags":["rlvr","grpo","policy-optimization","reasoning"],"links":{"arxiv":"https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08690","pdf":"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.08690","github":null,"project":null,"source_url":null}},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"In RLVR, outcome-only methods like GRPO are stable and strong, while theoretically appealing dense, fine-grained rewards/advantages (token- or step-level) often underperform in practice. The paper identifies why: Monte Carlo (MC) estimation of early-token advantages—by sampling multiple continuations from a prefix and averaging outcome rewards—has very high variance and frequent sign inconsistencies under realistic sampling budgets, making optimization unstable and worse than simply broadcasting the final outcome reward (GRPO).","importance":"This exposes a structural dilemma in RLVR credit assignment: fine-grained signals have a higher theoretical ceiling, but are statistically unreliable at feasible inference budgets. Resolving this is important for improving reasoning-process quality (not just final correctness) and achieving better performance under the same compute constraints.","technical_approach":"$49","experiments":"On math reasoning benchmarks, SKPO shows substantial gains over GRPO and improved OOD robustness. The analysis (e.g., Fig. 1) demonstrates that MC + group-relative advantage estimation produces high-variance, sign-flipping advantages for early tokens under practical budgets, explaining why dense approaches can be stably worse than outcome-only GRPO. Additional analysis reports higher intermediate-step quality (implicit advantage) for SKPO-trained models.","reading_guide":"must_read (deep dive): 1) Fig. 1 to internalize the core empirical finding: early-token MC advantages are noisy and sign-inconsistent. 2) Methodology/§3.1 for the formal token-level MC reward definition, the convergence-to-outcome property near the end of trajectories (motivating GRPO as a limiting case), and why sampling at a single intermediate point helps. 3) Fig. 2 to fully understand the upstream/downstream split, single-stream optimization, the [s,q] skip connection, and the single-pass rollout reuse. 4) §3.2 objectives to see why upstream avoids group-relative estimation while downstream retains it. 5) Experiments/ablations focusing on compute-matched statistically under limited sampling (high variance + sign errors), and a structural fix: two-phase optimization with MC applied at a single intermediate point—stable single-stream learning for upstream and GRPO-style stability for downstream—connected via [s,q] to transfer useful upstream reasoning without over-constraining exploration, all at roughly GRPO-level worse under realistic budgets (sign errors/variance), explaining GRPO’s robustness; run their variance/sign-consistency diagnostics internally before investing in finer-grained CA."}},{"id":"2604.08865","title":"SPPO: Sequence-Level PPO for Long-Horizon Reasoning Tasks","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-10T01:58:21+00:00","category_id":"post_train","cover_url":"/covers/2604_08865.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.AI"],"summary":{"core_problem":"长链路（长 CoT）推理的 RLVR 场景中，标准 token-level PPO 依赖 token-level critic + GAE 做时序信用分配，但在“超长时域 + 稀疏终局奖励”下会出现结构性不稳定：优势估计高偏差、critic 在序列尾部语义线索上过拟合导致 advantage 在关键位置塌缩（tail effect），训练易震荡/崩溃。与此同时，critic-free 的 GRPO 虽更稳，但需要每个 prompt 多采样 N>1 来构造组内基线，吞吐受限、计算开销大。","importance":"论文抓住了推理对齐里最核心的工程矛盾：稳定性（低偏差、低方差）与吞吐（少采样、低显存）难以兼得。它将 GRPO 的经验成功“理论化”为一种隐式的序列级 bandit 视角，并据此提出可扩展的替代算法，使得在不牺牲 PPO 的样本效率前提下获得接近 outcome-based 更新的稳定性，对大规模数学/逻辑推理 RLVR 训练具有直接指导意义。","technical_approach":"关键洞察：GRPO 的优势函数本质上在做“按 prompt 难度自适应缩放”的序列级基线，它等价于把整段回答当作一个原子动作来优化——即把 token-level MDP 隐式改写成 Sequence-Level Contextual Bandit（SL-CB）。\n\nSPPO 的做法是把这种隐式改写显式化：\n1) 任务重建模：将 prompt 视为静态 context，将整条 CoT/response 视为单个 action，时域折叠为 H=1，从根源上移除 token-level GAE 在长时域传播终局奖励带来的高偏差与“尾部过拟合”问题。\n2) 序列级 PPO 目标：在序列层面计算概率比（整段 response 的 logprob 之和形成序列级 ratio），用 PPO 的 clipped surrogate 做稳定更新，但 advantage 不再是逐 token 的 GAE，而是“终局回报 − 序列级价值基线”。\n3) 学习到的标量 value baseline：训练一个标量 V(prompt)（或 V(context)）来预测该 prompt 下的期望终局回报，用它替代 GRPO 需要多采样才能得到的组内均值/标准差基线，从而把方差压下去并允许 N=1 单样本更新。\n4) 计算/显存优化：提出 Decoupled Critic——用更小的 critic（如 1.5B）为更大的 policy（如 7B）提供序列级价值估计。由于价值函数从 token-level 变为标量、学习难度下降，critic 可显著轻量化，降低显存与训练成本（文中报告约 12.8% memory 降幅）。\n\n整体上，SPPO 试图在“PPO 的样本效率”与“GRPO 的 outcome 稳定性”之间取得折中：用显式序列级建模消除偏差源，用可泛化的标量 baseline 降低方差源，并用 N=1 提升吞吐。","experiments":"评测覆盖 AIME24/25、AMC23、MATH、Minerva 等稀疏可验证奖励的推理基准。主要结论：\n- 稳定性：SPPO 解决标准 PPO 的 value/advantage 塌缩与训练不稳定（与 Figure 1 所示 tail effect 对应）。\n- 性能：在峰值表现上可匹配 GRPO，但收敛更平滑、训练更稳。\n- 吞吐：由于不需要 GRPO 的多采样基线，SPPO 在相同设置下实现约 5.9× 训练速度提升（以训练吞吐/时间计）。\n- 资源：Decoupled Critic 方案在保持效果的同时降低显存占用（文中以 Figure 6 展示约 12.8%）。","reading_guide":"$4a","authors_note":"作者的核心立场是：推理对齐的关键不是“去掉 critic”，而是“去掉 token-level 时序分解”。GRPO 的有效性来自把整段推理当作原子动作并用 prompt 相关基线做归一化；SPPO 则把这一点显式化，并用可泛化的标量价值模型替代昂贵的多采样统计基线，从而在稳定性与吞吐之间取得更优折中。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Tianyi Wang","Yixia Li","Long Li","Yibiao Chen","Shaohan Huang","Yun Chen","Peng Li","Yang Liu","Guanhua Chen"],"notable_authors":[],"tags":["ppo","rlvr","long-horizon-reasoning","sequence-level-optimization","alignment"],"links":{"arxiv":"https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08865","pdf":"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.08865","github":null,"project":null,"source_url":null}},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"In long-horizon CoT RL with sparse terminal (verifiable) rewards, standard token-level PPO (token critic + GAE) becomes structurally unstable: credit assignment over thousands of tokens yields high bias, and the critic tends to overfit semantic cues near the sequence tail, causing the advantage to vanish exactly where learning signal is needed (“tail effect”). Critic-free GRPO is more stable but requires N>1 samples per prompt to build a group baseline, severely hurting throughput and compute efficiency.","importance":"The paper targets a central bottleneck in RLVR reasoning alignment: you typically trade stability for throughput. By reinterpreting GRPO’s empirical success as an implicit shift to a sequence-level contextual bandit view, the work proposes a scalable alternative that preserves PPO-like sample efficiency while achieving outcome-style stability—highly relevant for large-scale math/logic RL post-training.","technical_approach":"$4b","experiments":"Evaluations on AIME24/25, AMC23, MATH, and Minerva show:\n- Stability: SPPO avoids standard PPO’s value/advantage collapse associated with the tail effect.\n- Performance: matches GRPO’s peak accuracy with smoother convergence.\n- Throughput: achieves ~5.9× training speedup over GRPO by avoiding multi-sampling baselines.\n- Resources: Decoupled Critic reduces memory footprint (Figure 6 reports ~12.8%).","reading_guide":"$4c","authors_note":"The authors argue the key is not “removing the critic” but “removing token-level temporal decomposition.” GRPO succeeds because it implicitly optimizes at the sequence level with a prompt-dependent baseline; SPPO makes this explicit and replaces expensive multi-sample baselines with a generalizable scalar value model, enabling stable and high-throughput N=1 training."},"reading_tier":"must_read","recommendation":{"zh":"把“长时域+稀疏终奖”下 PPO 崩溃归因到 tail effect 并给出序列级替代，足以改变我对 RLVR 信用分配的 prior；建议立刻按其 ablation 复现稳定性/吞吐曲线。","en":"It cleanly pins PPO instability in long-horizon sparse-reward RLVR to a tail-effect failure mode and offers a sequence-level fix—this should update your credit-assignment prior; I’d immediately reproduce their stability/throughput ablations."}},{"id":"2604.08706","title":"Efficient RL Training for LLMs with Experience Replay","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-09T18:56:12+00:00","category_id":"post_train","cover_url":"/covers/2604_08706.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.LG"],"summary":{"core_problem":"LLM 的 RL 后训练（PPO/GRPO 等）普遍采用“尽量 on-policy”的 generate-then-discard：rollout 生成一次只用一次就丢弃。但在实际系统中生成（推理）成本极高，常占总 GPU 小时的 80%+，导致整体训练计算效率极差。社区普遍认为 replay 会因 off-policy（staleness）带来性能下降，因此很少系统研究在 LLM RL 中如何安全复用轨迹。","importance":"论文把“经验回放”从传统 RL 的常识带回 LLM RL 工程：当生成昂贵时，严格 on-policy 不是最优计算策略。它给出可操作的 buffer 设计与理论框架（staleness-variance、diversity、generation cost 的权衡），并用实证证明：合理 replay 能显著节省推理算力且不降性能，甚至提升 pass@k（多样性/稳定性带来的正则化效应）。这对任何以吞吐为瓶颈的 RLVR/RLAIF 管线都有直接价值。","technical_approach":"论文围绕“异步 RL 训练 + replay buffer”建立统一分析与工程实现。\n\n1) 系统设定（异步训练）：将 GPU 分为 inference workers（生成 rollout）与 trainers（反传更新）。两者权重可能不同步，天然存在一定 off-policy。传统做法是队列传输、用一次即丢。\n2) Replay Buffer 机制：inference 将 rollout 写入 buffer（可 FIFO 保留最近 N 条）；trainer 从 buffer 采样 batch，采样不删除，从而一条轨迹可被复用多次（replay ratio>1）。buffer 可按均匀采样，也可按 recency、reward、梯度范数、已采样次数等策略采样，并可设置衰减/淘汰规则。\n3) 理论框架（核心）：把“计算效率最优”形式化为 SGD 的 bias-variance 分解下的权衡：\n- staleness（越旧越 off-policy）会引入梯度偏差/方差增大；\n- buffer 过小会降低样本多样性、易过拟合；\n- 生成成本越高，复用带来的 compute 节省越大。\n论文推导 buffer size 与 replay ratio 的最优区间/趋势：当 inference 相对训练更贵时，最优策略会更偏向 replay（更高复用）。\n4) 实证策略探索：研究 buffer 大小、FIFO 深度、W/T（worker/trainer 比例）等对性能、稳定性、输出多样性（pass@k）与总 compute 的影响；并探索更“聪明”的采样（如优先正样本）与替代损失以扩大可稳定 replay 的范围。\n\n总体方法论：不把 on-policy 当教条，而是把“单位 compute 的性能”作为目标函数，寻找可控 off-policy 的最优点。","experiments":"在异步管线中以 Qwen2.5-7B 在 OpenR1-Math-220k 上系统扫描超参（buffer 容量、FIFO、采样策略、W/T 切分等），并在更大模型上验证可迁移性。主要发现：\n- 严格 on-policy 并非 compute 最优；适度 replay 可在不降最终准确率的情况下显著减少生成开销。\n- 合理 buffer 还能作为正则化稳定训练、保持输出多样性，某些设置下提升 pass@k。\n- 过度复用会因 staleness/多样性下降导致性能退化；存在“甜点区间”。\n- 计算收益：简单 buffer 策略可节省最高约 40% 总 compute，同时保持或略超 on-policy 基线最终表现（文中 Figure 1 等展示）。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读建议：详细技术分析 + reading_guide）\n- 重点章节：\n  1) Introduction：明确问题设定——推理成本主导 RL 后训练预算；挑战“必须严格 on-policy”的共识。\n  2) Experience Replay for Off-Policy RL：精读异步系统描述（W inference / T trainer）、buffer 的实现细节（FIFO、分片、采样不删除）以及它如何改变 compute 构成（trainer compute vs inference compute）。\n  3) 理论分析部分：重点看 trick），并在异步训练现实设定下讨论。\n  - 用理论把“严格 on-policy 非最优”说清楚：推理昂贵时应主动引入可控 off-policy。\n  - 发现 replay 可能提升多样性/稳定性（pass@k）这一反直觉现象，并给出可操作的采样/缓冲策略。\n\nskim（泛读建议：方法概述 + reading_guide）\n- 先读 Introduction + Figure RL post-training commonly follows a near on-policy “generate-then-discard” workflow: each rollout is generated once, used for a single update, then thrown away. But generation (inference) is extremely expensive in practice—often >80% of GPU hours—making this paradigm highly compute-inefficient. Experience replay is underused in LLM RL due to the belief that off-policy (stale) data inevitably hurts final performance.","importance":"The paper reintroduces experience replay as a first-class tool for LLM RL when generation dominates cost. It provides a principled framework and practical buffer designs showing that strict on-policy sampling is compute-suboptimal under expensive generation. Empirically, well-tuned replay can cut inference compute substantially without degrading—and sometimes improving—final accuracy and pass@k via stabilization/diversity effects.","technical_approach":"$4d","experiments":"Using Qwen2.5-7B on OpenR1-Math-220k in an asynchronous pipeline, the paper performs extensive sweeps over buffer size, FIFO depth, replay ratio, W/T splits, and sampling strategies, and validates findings on larger models. Key results:\n- Strict on-policy is not compute-optimal; moderate replay can reduce generation cost without hurting final accuracy.\n- A properly sized buffer can stabilize training and preserve/improve output diversity, sometimes improving pass@k.\n- Over-aggressive reuse degrades performance due to staleness/diversity loss; there is a clear “sweet spot.”\n- Compute gains: simple replay strategies can save up to ~40% total compute while matching or slightly exceeding on-policy baselines (e.g., Figure 1).","reading_guide":"$4e","authors_note":"The intended shift is from maximizing performance per step to maximizing performance per unit of compute. Models","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-03-17T02:24:37+00:00","category_id":"post_train","cover_url":"/covers/2604_08557.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CL","cs.AI"],"summary":{"core_problem":"论文研究扩散语言模型（dLLM）安全对齐的一个“承重假设”：一旦在去噪过程中提交（commit）的 token（尤其是拒答 token）就不可逆、永久固定。作者证明该假设在推理时可被“轨迹级”操控绕过：在模型早期已经提交拒答词后，攻击者将这些已提交位置重新置为 [MASK]（re-mask），再注入极短的肯定/服从前缀（prefix），即可把后续去噪轨迹从拒答重定向到合规输出。","importance":"意义在于把 dLLM 的安全脆弱性从“输入级提示词对抗”提升到“推理轨迹级不变量被破坏”的层面：现有对齐方法（SFT、偏好优化/VRPO 等）默认而未显式约束“提交不可逆”，导致安全信号高度前置且可被擦除。该结果对即将/已经部署的 dLLM（文中以 Mercury 2 商用为背景）是直接的系统性风险：即使提示词层面很安全，只要推理管线允许中间态被改写（或被插件/代理/服务端组件间接影响），就可能高成功率越狱。","technical_approach":"方法为 TrajHijack（首个 dLLM 轨迹级攻击）。核心由两个不可替代的组件构成：\n1) Re-mask committed refusals：在去噪前 k 步（典型 8–16/64）模型已高置信提交“sorry/cannot”等拒答 token 后，攻击者定位这些拒答位置并强制重置为 [MASK]，显式违反作者称为 Monotonicity Assumption（提交单调不可逆）。\n2) Prefix injection（compliance anchoring）：在恢复去噪前插入一个很短的肯定/服从前缀（例如 8-token 通用合规前缀），作为“锚”改变后续双向条件化（bidirectional conditioning）下的全局一致性收敛方向，使模型不再回到拒答轨迹。\n机制解释：作者提出 Early Commitment Effect（安全对齐在早期步数就以高置信拒答 token 形式被“写死”），而 dLLM 的不可逆提交使这些 token 后续不再被重新评估；一旦攻击者抹掉这些早期拒答 token，再用前缀提供新的高层语用约束，后续去噪会在全序列一致性压力下生成合规内容。\n此外作者给出若干概念化总结：Compliance Anchoring、Bidirectional Conditioning Advantage，并提出 Coverage–Dominance–Provenance 条件框架来组织可检验预测。\n一个重要“负结果”：作者实现了可微的 Gumbel-softmax 链式梯度优化（回应先前工作称其不可解），但发现梯度优化反而稳定降低 ASR，说明该漏洞不需要复杂优化，且“更聪明的优化”未必更强。","experiments":"主要实验结论（以 HarmBench 为核心评测）：\n- TrajHijack 在三种公开安全微调 dLLM 上实现 74–82% ASR；使用通用 8-token 合规前缀可达 92–98% ASR。\n- “两组件不可约”：仅 re-mask 几乎无效（约 4.4% ASR），仅 prefix 也几乎无效（约 5.7% ASR），组合才显著成功。\n- 泛化性：跨 SFT 与偏好优化（VRPO）模型均有效，且不需要梯度/不需要目标有害答案。\n- 防御相关：作者指出 DiffuGuard 的单调性检测对该攻击检出率仅约 14%，原因是 prefix 注入可抵消 mask 数变化；并提出 Defense Inversion Effect：某些输出级防御（如 A2D）反而提高 ASR（文中示例 89.9% vs 76.1%），表明仅在输出端做过滤/改写无法覆盖轨迹级操控。","reading_guide":"$4f","authors_note":"作者的核心立场是：dLLM 安全并非主要败在“提示词太狡猾”，而是败在推理过程的单调不可逆设计与对齐信号的早期前置之间的结构性耦合；因此防御应上移到“轨迹不变量与中间态完整性”层面，而不是继续堆叠输入/输出侧的补丁。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Arth Singh"],"notable_authors":[],"tags":["diffusion-lm","jailbreak","alignment","sampling-schedule","harmbench"],"links":{"arxiv":"https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08557","pdf":"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.08557","github":null,"project":null,"source_url":null}},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"The paper targets a load-bearing assumption in safety-aligned diffusion language models (dLLMs): once a token is committed during denoising, it is permanent. The authors show that if an attacker violates this monotonicity at inference time—by re-masking already-committed refusal tokens and injecting a short affirmative/compliance prefix—the denoising trajectory can be redirected from refusal to compliance, yielding high jailbreak success.","importance":"It reframes dLLM safety failures from prompt-level adversarial inputs to trajectory-level violations of inference invariants. Current alignment (SFT, VRPO/preference optimization, token-level training) implicitly relies on commitment irreversibility without enforcing robustness to intermediate-state tampering. This is a deployment-critical risk: even with safe prompting, any system that allows intermediate denoising states to be modified (directly or via tooling/pipelines) can be reliably jailbroken.","technical_approach":"$50","experiments":"Key results (HarmBench):\n- TrajHijack achieves 74–82% attack success rate (ASR) across three public safety-tuned dLLMs; with a generic 8-token compliance prefix, ASR rises to 92–98%.\n- Two-component irreducibility: re-masking alone (~4.4% ASR) and prefix alone (~5.7% ASR) largely fail; the combination is necessary.\n- Generalization: works across SFT and VRPO models; requires no gradients and no full harmful target response.\n- Defense findings: DiffuGuard’s monotonicity check detects the attack poorly (~14%) because prefix injection offsets mask-count changes; output-level defenses can backfire (Defense Inversion Effect), e.g., A2D increases ASR (89.9% vs 76.1%), indicating output-side patching is insufficient for trajectory-level attacks.","reading_guide":"$51","authors_note":"The authors’ thesis is that dLLM safety fragility is structural: it arises from coupling early refusal commitment with an assumed irreversible denoising schedule. The authors propose multilingual story moral generation—given a story summary, generate a short moral/lesson—and evaluate models against human moral distributions across language–culture contexts.","importance":"It shifts alignment evaluation from static knowledge or rule-following to culturally grounded narrative interpretation: abstracting from plot details to normative lessons, where cross-cultural variation is expected. learning with verifiable rewards，可验证奖励强化学习）的模型在“可验证目标任务”（如数学推理）上对persona变化表现出系统性鲁棒；而SFT/蒸馏等非RLVR后训练配方更persona敏感。为量化鲁棒性，提出Persona Stability Score (PSS)：基于同一模型在多persona集合上的任务表现分布来度量“跨persona稳定性”（越接近1越稳定）。同时作者指出RLVR带来一个权衡：在目标可验证的任务上，RLVR倾向于压缩与persona相关的行为差异（更稳定），但在需要强角色扮演/风格表达的场景会削弱persona fidelity（不太“入戏”）。在此基础上提出PerMix-RLVR：一种训练策略，目标是在保留RLVR带来的“对有害persona变化的鲁棒性”的同时，在需要时恢复persona表达力。其思想可概括为：在RLVR对齐框架中引入“persona混合/分配”的训练设计，让模型既学会对任务目标保持稳定，又在特定persona条件下保留可控的风格/角色差异（论文声称在数学与role-playing任务上优于标准RLVR）。","experiments":"宏观对比实验：作者基于公开后训练模型做跨家族观察（Qwen3、Llama3.1/3.2、Gemma3等），在MATH500与AIME2024上用固定的16个system personas（覆盖STEM专家、教育水平、性格特质、职业角色）评测，并用PSS衡量persona稳定性。观察到：包含RLVR的模型（如Qwen3-32B）相对更persona-stable；非RLVR管线模型更敏感。论文还声称在后续受控实验中验证该趋势，并展示“鲁棒性—fidelity”权衡，以及PerMix-RLVR在数学推理与角色扮演任务上的改进（相对标准RLVR）。","reading_guide":"must_read（精读）：1) 1（persona试错成本与波动直观展示）、以及展示不同模型家族在多persona下性能分布/方差或PSS对比的图；4) PerMix-RLVR方法段：精读其训练目标如何同时约束“可验证任务的稳定性”和“角色表达力恢复”，以及与标准RLVR的差异；5) Ablation/控制实验：关注是否控制了模型规模、数据、解码策略、persona模板等混杂因素。\nskim（泛读）：1) paper studies the volatility of persona prompting: the same LLM can perform very differently under different persona/system-role prompts, making the “best persona” hard to predict and forcing costly inference-time prompt trial-and-error. The authors ask whether persona sensitivity is driven by post-training objectives, and whether we can train models to be robust to persona variations while still preserving persona expressivity/fidelity when role-playing is desired.","importance":"Persona prompting is widely used for steering style and improving instruction performance, but its high variance creates real deployment costs and reliability risks. Training-time persona robustness could reduce prompt engineering and evaluation overhead. At the same time, if alignment methods like RLVR reduce persona expressivity, we need training strategies that explicitly balance task stability and controllable role-playing fidelity.","technical_approach":"Key finding and framing: models post-trained with RLVR (reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards) become systematically more robust to persona variations on verifiable-goal tasks (e.g., math), compared to non-RLVR recipes such as SFT or distillation. The paper introduces Persona Stability Score (PSS) to quantify how much task performance varies across a fixed persona set (higher is more stable). The authors further identify a robustness–fidelity trade-off: RLVR improves stability on goal-oriented/verifiable tasks but attenuates persona fidelity in role-playing settings. To address this, they propose PerMix-RLVR, a training strategy intended to retain RLVR’s robustness to harmful persona variation while recovering persona expressivity when needed, by incorporating persona-mixing/training design within the RLVR alignment framework (claimed to outperform standard RLVR on both math reasoning and role-playing tasks).","experiments":"Macro-level evaluation on publicly available post-trained models across families (Qwen3, Llama3.1/3.2, Gemma3) using MATH500 and AIME2024. Observations: RLVR-including pipelines (e.g., Qwen3-32B) show higher persona stability; non-RLVR pipelines are more persona-sensitive. The paper also reports controlled experiments validating the trend, demonstrating the robustness–fidelity trade-off, and showing PerMix-RLVR improvements over standard RLVR on math and role-playing benchmarks.","reading_guide":"must_read: (1) Introduction for the motivation and the shift from inference-time persona search to training-time robustness; (2) “RLVR Alignment and Persona Robustness & Fidelity” for the PSS definition, persona set design, and the evidence for the robustness–fidelity trade-off; (3) Key figures: Figure 1 for the cost/volatility intuition, plus plots/tables comparing performance distributions or PSS across model families; (4) PerMix-RLVR section for the exact training objective/procedure and how it differs from vanilla RLVR; (5) Controlled experiments/ablations to check confounders (scale, data, decoding, persona templates).\nskim: read Introduction + contributions, skim PSS and the public-model comparison, then jump to PerMix-RLVR’s main idea and headline results (math + role-play).","authors_note":"The authors argue persona sensitivity is not random but strongly tied to post-training alignment objectives. distillation：为避免推理时依赖外部组件，用冲突检测器+SMT求解器从Alpaca自动构造层级指令数据集，每条样本带“求解器选出的适用指令集”标注；再用hierarchy-aware目标进行微调，在标准监督之外加入“层级语义损失（hierarchical semantic paper targets hierarchical instruction-following under multiple heterogeneous instruction sources (system policies, user requests, tool outputs, retrieved context, chat history) that often partially Prior work emphasizes adversarial prompt-injection settings; this work focuses on resolving common non-adversarial conflicts while preserving utility and behavioral consistency under an explicit authority hierarchy.","importance":"Real-world LLM applications (agents, tool use, RAG, long-context assistants) inherently mix instructions with different authority levels. A Reflexive Audit of Self-Stated Safety Policies","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-10T10:18:45+00:00","category_id":"post_train","cover_url":"/covers/2604_09189.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CL","cs.AI","cs.LG"],"summary":{"core_problem":"论文研究一个“反身性(reflexive)”安全一致性问题：同一个LLM在被要求“精确描述自己的安全边界/规则”时所陈述的政策（self-stated policy），是否与它在真实有害请求基准上的实际行为一致。现有评测多用外部标准衡量“是否安全”，但不衡量“是否遵守自己声称的规则”，因此无法发现“模型自我承诺—行为执行”之间的系统性断裂。","importance":"重要性在于：1）安全对齐往往通过RLHF等隐式过程形成，缺少可检视的“规则书”，而部署与治理却越来越依赖模型自述、系统提示词、政策文档等显式表述；2）若模型在自述中宣称“绝对拒绝”但在轻微改写/语境变化下仍会提供帮助，这类“自我违规”会削弱可审计性与合规可信度；3）该工作提供一种不依赖外部规范、而是以模型自我陈述为基准的可量化一致性指标，可补齐现有安全评测维度。","technical_approach":"提出Symbolic-Neural Consistency Audit (SNCA) 三阶段框架，并强调严格信息隔离：Phase 1规则抽取、Phase 2行为测试互不泄露，Phase 3全确定性零LLM调用。\n1）规则抽取：对每个(模型,危害类别)用结构化5问提示在新对话中让模型“精确描述自己的安全政策”，覆盖默认行为(Q1)、拒绝条件(Q2)、允许条件(Q3)、对虚构/专业等框架敏感性(Q4)、单句政策声明(Q5)。多次运行以避免随机拒答，选取最长的非错误回复作为代表。\n2）规则形式化与类型化：用独立judge模型J基于Q1–Q5将自述政策归为可测试的类型谓词：Absolute（无例外拒绝，∀x∈C:refuse(x)）、Conditional（满足条件则可协助，否则拒绝，cond→comply; ¬cond→refuse）、Adaptive（条件+表面框架共同决定，cond∧frame→comply）、Opaque（过于含糊无法形成可检验谓词；不计入一致性得分但统计不透明率）。该“类型谓词分类”是把自然语言政策转为可审计符号约束的关键。\n3）行为合规评估：在中性系统提示下对同一模型跑危害基准请求（与Phase 1完全隔离），固定解码温度收集回答；再用两级分类器判定每条回答是REFUSE/COMPLY/PARTIAL：Tier1为确定性关键词拒绝短语规则；对“拒绝语言+实质内容”标为PARTIAL等。最后将行为标签与Phase 1得到的谓词进行确定性比对，得到Symbolic-Neural Consistency Score (SNCS)：模型自述规则中被其行为实际遵守的比例；同时报告Opaque rate作为“可陈述性/可审计性”维度。","experiments":"在4个前沿模型、45个危害类别上评测，共47,496条观测。核心发现包括：\n1）系统性“自述—行为”缺口：即便模型声称Absolute拒绝，也常在基准请求上出现合规或部分合规，表明自我承诺并不可靠。\n2）架构/推理范式影响一致性：推理型模型在其能清晰陈述的规则上SNCS更高（文中给出可达~0.80的量级），但更容易出现政策“不可判定/不可形式化”的Opaque（约29%不透明率），呈现“一致性 vs 可陈述性”的权衡；非推理模型几乎能对所有类别给出可分类政策，但遵守度更低（SNCS约0.25–0.55）。\n3）跨模型政策收敛性弱：仅约11%的危害类别在四个模型间得到相同的规则类型，说明“安全对齐”并未收敛到共享的隐式政策边界。\n（注：以上数值与结论来自论文摘要与引言中披露的关键统计。）","reading_guide":"must_read（精读）：\n- 重点读Method: SNCA Framework：三阶段信息隔离、5问抽取设计、为何需要多次抽取取最长回复。\n- 重点掌握“类型谓词”四分类（Absolute/Conditional/Adaptive/Opaque）及其形式化谓词写法，这是全文创新核心。\n- 精读行为分类与确定性比对：两级分类器如何把自由文本回答映射到REFUSE/COMPLY/PARTIAL，以及SNCS如何计算；关注PARTIAL在一致性判定中的处理。\n- 看Figure 1（管线示例）与实验主表：对比不同模型的SNCS与Opaque rate，理解“推理模型高一致但高不透明”的结论如何由数据支撑。\n- 创新点抓手：反身性审计（同一模型既写规则又被审计）、符号化可检验谓词、将“不透明率”作为独立维度。\n\nskim（泛读）：\n- 读Introduction把握问题动机：外部基准 vs 自我一致性缺口。\n- 快读方法概览：三阶段+四类谓词+SNCS定义。\n- 直接看实验结论段与关键统计（SNCS区间、29% Opaque、11%一致类别）获取主要takeaways。\n- 若时间有限，只需看Figure 1与结果对比图/表即可建立直觉。","authors_note":"作者强调SNCA并不声称恢复模型“潜在真实内在政策”，而是把“模型在被要求精确自述时愿意公开承诺的政策”作为可测代理；并通过严格信息隔离与确定性Phase 3避免评测污染。论文将“能否清晰陈述可检验规则（Opacity）”与“是否遵守自述规则（SNCS）”区分为两条独立的对齐质量轴。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Avni Mittal"],"notable_authors":[],"tags":["safety","alignment","RLHF","consistency","evaluation"],"links":{"arxiv":"https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09189","pdf":"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.09189","github":null,"project":null,"source_url":null}},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"The paper studies a reflexive safety-consistency question: does an LLM’s behavior on harmful-request benchmarks match the safety rules it explicitly states when asked to precisely describe its own boundaries? Prior safety evaluations mostly compare models to external norms, but they do not test whether a model follows its self-declared policy—thus missing “self-violation” failures where the model claims strict refusal yet complies under mild rephrasing or contextual framing.","importance":"Why it matters: (1) RLHF-style alignment yields implicit, hard-to-inspect policies, while deployment and governance increasingly rely on explicit self-descriptions (system prompts, documentation, self-regulation); (2) mismatches between stated commitments and actual behavior undermine auditability, compliance, and trust; (3) the work adds a complementary evaluation axis—self-consistency—without requiring an externally specified rulebook.","technical_approach":"$54","experiments":"They evaluate 4 frontier models over 45 harm categories with 47,496 observations. Key findings reported in the abstract/introduction: (1) systematic gaps between stated policy and observed behavior—models that claim absolute refusal often still comply; (2) architecture matters: reasoning models achieve higher SNCS on articulable rules (up to ~0.80 scale) but exhibit substantial policy opacity (~29% Opaque), revealing a consistency–articulability trade-off; non-reasoning models articulate policies across categories but follow them less reliably (SNCS ~0.25–0.55); (3) cross-model policy agreement is low—only ~11% of harm categories receive the same rule type across all four models, suggesting safety alignment does not converge to a shared implicit boundary.","reading_guide":"$55","authors_note":"The authors explicitly note SNCA does not claim access to a model’s latent “true internal policy.” Instead, it operationalizes a measurable proxy: the policy the model is willing to explicitly articulate under structured prompting. stage to avoid evaluation contamination."},"reading_tier":"skim","recommendation":{"zh":"把“模型自述规则”当内生基准做审计，能直接指导你写更可测的 policy prompt；只看指标定义和最典型的自我违约案例即可。","en":"Audits models against their own stated paper centers on credit assignment (CA) in reinforcement learning for LLMs: when rewards are sparse and outcome-level (e.g., final-answer correctness or task completion), how to attribute credit/blame to specific actions within very long trajectories—tokens, reasoning steps, tool calls, or dialogue turns. The CA problem becomes severe in two regimes: reasoning RL (single ultra-long chain-of-thought generations, ~500 to 30K+ tokens) and agentic RL (multi-turn environment interaction with stochastic transitions, partial observability, 100+ turns, ~100K–1M tokens), where episode-level signals become increasingly uninformative.","importance":"Why it matters: (1) RL has powered recent leaps in both reasoning models and LLM agents, but both are bottlenecked by coarse terminal rewards; (2) as horizons grow and environments become stochastic, assigning the same advantage to all actions dilutes learning signals, hurting sample efficiency and stability; (3) a systematic CA-focused map helps researchers choose methods under different constraints (compute, auxiliary models, supervision) and motivates standardized reporting and evaluation protocols.","technical_approach":"$56","experiments":"As a survey, the primary “evidence” is literature aggregation and cross-paper comparison rather than a single new algorithm validated by large-scale training runs. Optimization with Fewer Prompts","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-09T22:31:15+00:00","category_id":"post_train","cover_url":"/covers/2604_08801.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.LG","cs.CL"],"summary":{"core_problem":"论文研究“为什么系统提示词（system prompt）的自动优化在不同任务上效果极不稳定”。作者将提示词优化视为RL问题：策略生成候选system prompt，用冻结LLM在数据集上的准确率作奖励；核心问题是：何时存在足够清晰的优化信号、何时信号会被生成随机性与数据异质性淹没，从而导致“算力堆不出更好prompt”。","importance":"系统提示词是当前LLM对齐/能力释放的关键接口，且无需改权重，成本低、可迁移。但实践中prompt优化常常“玄学”：有的任务一优化就涨，有的任务几乎不动。本文给出可解释的判据（奖励方差分解与信号强弱条件）以及一个反直觉结论（更多训练user prompts可能更差），并据此提出用更少样本反而更有效的过滤训练方法p1，对推理类异质数据尤其重要。","technical_approach":"1) RL式prompt优化设定：冻结基础模型π，仅训练system prompt生成策略π'（meta-prompt s条件下生成x'），奖励r(x,y)为二值正确性；采用on-policy GRPO变体（无KL到参考策略、无std advantage归一化），用V^{π'_t}(s)=E_{x'~π'_t}[r(x')]作baseline。\n2) 关键分析：将“不同system prompt下的奖励方差”分解为两部分——(a) response variance：同一system prompt下因采样/推理随机性导致的回报波动；(b) prompt variance：不同system prompt真实期望回报差异。结论：当prompt variance足够大（相对response variance占主导）时，RL能获得稳定梯度信号并成功；当response variance主导时，优化信号被噪声淹没，prompt优化难以推进（典型如复杂数学推理）。\n3) 反直觉现象：扩大训练集（更多user prompts）会降低prompt variance。原因是不同user prompt对system prompt的偏好可能相互抵消；在异质任务（如数学推理）中，“对某题有帮助的prompt”可能对另一题有害，平均后候选prompt的期望回报趋同，导致统计上难区分。\n4) 方法p1：用户提示过滤（user-prompt filtering）。不在全量训练集上优化，而是选取一小部分“能最大区分system prompt优劣”的user prompts——即在候选system prompts上表现出高奖励方差的样本子集。用该子集训练可显著增强优化信号；并且因为子集更“判别性”，所需训练样本更少但泛化更好。","experiments":"论文在指令遵循与推理两类基准上对比标准prompt优化与p1过滤训练：\n- 现象验证：在IFBench等较同质的instruction-following任务上，system prompt对奖励敏感，prompt variance较大，常规优化有效；在AIME等复杂推理上，response variance更大，常规优化即使算力增加也难提升。\n- 规模效应验证：增加user prompts数量会削弱prompt variance并伤害优化，尤其在异质推理数据上更明显。\n- p1效果：在推理数据上，过滤后显著提升；特别地，仅用AIME 24中“两个”user prompts训练得到的system prompt即可泛化到其他推理基准。\n- 迁移与跨模型：在Qwen3-4B-Instruct-2507上优化出的system prompt可迁移提升更大模型Qwen3-30B-A3B-Instruct-2507，并能提升训练未见的额外推理基准（文中Fig.1展示）。","reading_guide":"【skim（泛读）】\n- 先读Introduction：抓住两条主线结论——(i) 奖励方差=响应噪声+prompt差异；(ii) 数据越大可能越难优化；以及p1“少样本更强”的动机。\n- 再读Problem Setup：明确RL对象是谁（π'生成system prompt）、奖励如何定义、为何用GRPO变体。\n- 重点扫Fig.1：看跨模型/跨基准迁移的核心证据。\n\n【must_read（精读）】\n- 精读“Prompt Learnability/方差分解与可学性判据”相关章节：理解prompt variance与response variance的定义、估计方式、以及它们如何决定RL梯度信噪比。\n- 精读“更多user prompts为何更差”的分析与实验：这是本文最反直觉但最具指导意义的结论，直接影响你如何构造prompt优化数据集。\n- 精读p1算法细节：过滤指标如何计算（基于候选system prompts的奖励方差）、过滤后训练流程如何与GRPO结合、为何能在极小样本下泛化。\n- 对照关键图表：\n  1) 展示两类方差占比随任务变化的图（用于建立“何时可优化”的直觉）；\n  2) 数据规模vs prompt variance/性能曲线（用于理解“越多越差”）；\n  3) p1在AIME/推理基准上的提升与迁移图（用于验证方法有效性与外推）。","authors_note":"作者的核心观点是：prompt优化不是“总能work”的黑盒搜索，而是一个受统计信号支配的学习问题。成功的前提是system prompt之间存在可观的真实期望差异（prompt variance），且该差异不能被生成随机性（response variance）与跨样本偏好抵消所掩盖。p1的实用启示是：与其盲目扩大训练集，不如挑选最能区分prompt优劣的少量样本来放大优化信号，从而用更少prompt获得更好的prompt。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Zhaolin Gao","Yu","Wang","Bo Liu","Thorsten Joachims","Kianté Brantley","Wen Sun"],"notable_authors":["Thorsten Joachims"],"tags":["prompt-optimization","variance-decomposition","instruction-selection","black-box-optimization","robustness"],"links":{"arxiv":"https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08801","pdf":"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.08801","github":null,"project":null,"source_url":null}},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"The paper asks why automatic system-prompt optimization (via RL over prompts with a frozen LLM) is highly inconsistent across tasks. It studies when there exists a learnable optimization signal versus when the signal is drowned by generation stochasticity and dataset heterogeneity, making prompt optimization stall even with large compute.","importance":"System prompts are a low-cost, weight-free control interface for LLMs and can yield large gains, yet prompt optimization often behaves unpredictably. This work provides an explanatory criterion (a variance decomposition that characterizes signal vs noise), reveals a counterintuitive scaling failure mode (more training user prompts can hurt), and proposes a simple fix (p1 filtering) that improves optimization while using fewer prompts—especially impactful for heterogeneous reasoning tasks.","technical_approach":"$58","experiments":"The paper evaluates standard prompt optimization vs p1 on instruction-following and reasoning benchmarks:\n- Validates the variance story: instruction-following (e.g., IFBench) shows high sensitivity to system prompts (large prompt variance), enabling effective optimization; complex reasoning (e.g., AIME) is dominated by response variance, causing optimization to stagnate.\n- Demonstrates the scaling pitfall: adding more user prompts can dilute prompt variance and degrade optimization, especially on heterogeneous reasoning datasets.\n- Shows p1 gains: filtering yields substantial improvements on reasoning; notably, training on only two prompts from AIME 24 produces a system prompt that generalizes to other reasoning benchmarks.\n- Transfer: prompts optimized on Qwen3-4B-Instruct-2507 also improve a larger Qwen3-30B-A3B-Instruct-2507 and boost additional unseen reasoning benchmarks (highlighted in Fig. 1).","reading_guide":"$59","authors_note":"The central message is that prompt optimization is a statistical learning problem governed by signal (true expected differences among system prompts) versus noise (stochastic responses and heterogeneity-induced cancellation). When prompt variance is small, RL over prompts has little to learn. p1 operationalizes this insight by selecting a few highly discriminative user prompts to amplify the signal, often outperforming full-dataset training while using fewer prompts."},"reading_tier":"skim","recommendation":{"zh":"把 prompt 优化失败归因到奖励信号强弱而非“玄学”，并给出“样本更少更好”的可操作过滤；只看信号分解推导和 p1 过滤策略。","en":"Explains prompt-optimization instability via reward-signal strength (not mysticism) and gives an actionable “fewer samples can win” filter; read the signal decomposition and the p1 filtering rule."}},{"id":"2604.09529","title":"VL-Calibration: Decoupled Confidence Calibration for Large Vision-Language Models Reasoning","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-10T17:47:19+00:00","category_id":"post_train","cover_url":"/covers/2604_09529.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.CV","cs.AI","cs.CL"],"summary":{"core_problem":"论文解决LVLM（大视觉语言模型）在多模态推理中“答错但很自信”的校准问题，尤其是幻觉（hallucination）导致的高置信错误。作者指出：沿用文本LLM的“单一整体置信度+答案对错二值监督”的口径不适配LVLM，因为错误可能来自两类不同源头——视觉感知失败（没看对图/没grounding）或在感知正确前提下的推理错误；单一置信度会混淆两者，并且视觉不确定性常被语言先验掩盖。","importance":"在医疗、法律等高风险场景，模型不仅要“尽量对”，还要“知道自己何时不确定”。LVLM的错误往往是视觉幻觉或语言先验主导下的臆断，导致置信度严重失真。本文提出将置信度显式解耦为“视觉感知置信度”和“推理置信度”，并给出在缺乏视觉置信度真值标签时可训练的RL奖励构造与token级训练技巧，在降低ECE的同时还能提升准确率，具有直接工程价值。","technical_approach":"1) 置信度解耦框架（两阶段/两类token）：模型输出不仅包含推理链z与答案y，还显式生成与“视觉依据（visual rationale）”相关的置信度token，以及与“逻辑推理链（reasoning chain）”相关的置信度token，从而把不确定性来源拆开。\n2) RL训练范式：在RLVR（可验证奖励RL）基础上，除二值正确性奖励R_acc外，引入校准目标。对比既有方法（如用Brier Score对整体置信度c做L2校准），本文强调LVLM需要针对视觉与推理分别校准。\n3) 视觉置信度无真值的奖励估计：提出Visual Certainty Reward，将两类信号结合：\n  - Visual Grounding：比较“原图”与“扰动图”条件下模型输出分布的KL散度；KL越大表示输出对视觉内容更敏感、更grounded。\n  - Internal Certainty：对视觉描述相关token计算熵（entropy）；熵越低表示内部更确定。\n  - 融合方式：用log-scale形式整合，既奖励“既grounded又自信”的视觉表述，又通过对数压缩动态范围提升RL稳定性。\n4) Token-level Advantage Reweighting：指出二值结果奖励对所有token一视同仁会放大幻觉。作者用上述视觉不确定性估计对优势函数做token级重加权：对高视觉不确定且带来负优势的token加大惩罚，从而抑制不grounded的幻觉，同时尽量保留有效的视觉感知内容。","experiments":"在13个基准上系统评测（以Qwen3-VL系列为主）：\n- 校准指标：ECE显著下降（文中报告从0.421降至0.098）。\n- 准确率：在最强基线之上平均提升约2.3%–3.0%，表明校准训练未以牺牲能力为代价，反而改善推理/回答质量。\n- 泛化与鲁棒性：跨模型尺度、不同架构、以及OOD基准均观察到一致收益，支持“解耦校准+视觉确定性奖励+token级重加权”的通用性。","reading_guide":"【skim（泛读）】\n- 读Introduction：抓住动机（LVLM错误来源解耦）与三项贡献（解耦置信度、视觉确定性奖励、token级优势重加权）。\n- 读Methodology中对比段：理解与SaySelf/RLCR等“整体置信度+Brier”的差异。\n- 快看实验总表：ECE与Accuracy的同时提升是本文最重要的结果。\n\n【must_read（精读）】\n- 精读“Visual Certainty Reward”构造：\n  1) 原图vs扰动图KL作为grounding度量的合理性与实现细节；\n  2) 视觉描述token熵作为internal certainty的定义；\n  3) log-scale融合为何能稳定训练。\n- 精读“Token-level Advantage Reweighting”：这是把“视觉不确定性估计”真正注入RL优化的关键机制，决定是否能抑制幻觉而不伤害有效感知。\n- 精读消融实验：分别去掉grounding项/entropy项/log-scale/重加权，观察ECE与准确率如何变化，以确认每个组件的必要性。\n- 重点图表建议：\n  1) 框架示意图（两阶段解耦输出）；\n  2) ECE下降与可靠性图（reliability diagram，如有）；\n  3) OOD与跨尺度结果表（验证泛化）。","authors_note":"作者的关键洞察是：LVLM的“自信错误”往往不是单一原因，必须把视觉感知与逻辑推理的不确定性拆开表达与优化；否则语言先验会主导整体置信度。由于视觉置信度缺乏标注，论文用“对图像扰动的敏感性（grounding）+内部熵（certainty）”构造可学习的视觉确定性奖励，并进一步用token级优势重加权把该信号精细注入训练，从而同时改善校准与准确率。"},"metadata":{"institutions":[],"authors":["Wenyi Xiao","Xinchi Xu","Leilei Gan"],"notable_authors":[],"tags":["calibration","RLHF","VLM","uncertainty","hallucination"],"links":{"arxiv":"https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09529","pdf":"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.09529","github":null,"project":null,"source_url":null}},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"The paper tackles confidence miscalibration in large vision-language models (LVLMs), where models often produce incorrect or hallucinated answers with high certainty. It argues that text-LLM-style calibration—optimizing a single holistic confidence score using binary answer correctness—mismatches LVLMs because errors can stem from (i) visual perception/grounding failures or (ii) reasoning failures given correct perception; a single confidence conflates these sources and visual uncertainty is often overwhelmed by language priors.","importance":"In high-stakes applications, models must be both accurate and reliably uncertain when they are likely wrong. LVLM hallucinations and language-prior dominance make confidence particularly unreliable. By explicitly decoupling perception vs reasoning confidence and providing an RL-trainable visual-certainty signal without ground-truth confidence labels, the work offers a practical path to safer LVLM deployment, achieving large ECE reductions while improving accuracy.","technical_approach":"$5a","experiments":"Evaluated on 13 benchmarks (notably on Qwen3-VL models):\n- Calibration: ECE drops substantially (reported from 0.421 to 0.098).\n- Accuracy: improves by ~2.3%–3.0% over the strongest baselines, indicating calibration training also enhances answer quality.\n- Generalization: consistent gains across model scales, architectures, and out-of-distribution benchmarks, supporting the robustness of the decoupled calibration paradigm and the proposed rewards/training tricks.","reading_guide":"【skim】\n- Read the Introduction for motivation (perception vs reasoning error sources) and the three main contributions (decoupling, visual-certainty reward, token-level reweighting).\n- Skim the Methodology comparison to SaySelf/RLCR-style holistic confidence + Brier score.\n- Check the main results tables: simultaneous ECE reduction and accuracy gain is the headline.\n\n【must_read】\n- Study the Visual Certainty Reward in detail: KL(original vs perturbed) as grounding, entropy as internal certainty, and why log-scale fusion stabilizes RL.\n- Study Token-level Advantage Reweighting: the key mechanism that injects visual-uncertainty signals into optimization to curb hallucinations.\n- Read ablations: remove grounding/entropy/log-scale/reweighting to verify each component’s contribution.\n- Focus figures/tables: framework diagram (two-phase decoupling), calibration/reliability plots (if provided), and OOD + cross-scale results.","authors_note":"The main insight is that LVLM overconfidence is multi-causal; calibration must separate visual perception uncertainty from reasoning uncertainty. Lacking ground-truth visual-confidence labels, the paper constructs a learnable visual-certainty reward from image-perturbation sensitivity (grounding) and token entropy (internal certainty), and further applies token-level advantage reweighting to directly suppress ungrounded hallucination tokens—yielding better calibration and higher accuracy."},"reading_tier":"skim","recommendation":{"zh":"把 LVLM 置信度拆成“视觉感知 vs 推理”两头，工程上能直接降高置信幻觉；重点看解耦训练目标与无视觉真值时的奖励构造，别纠结花哨指标。","en":"Decouples LVLM confidence into perception vs 的可持续提升。","importance":"TIR 是面向真实应用（搜索、代码解释器、规划代理）的关键能力。训练范式若在早期就陷入无效探索或模式退化，会显著抬高算力与数据成本；若后期低熵坍塌，则限制上限。该工作提出“warm-up 但不重 SFT”的中间路线，目标是用更少合成数据获得更高 ROI（数据/训练/性能综合效率），对可扩展 agentic RL Policy Optimization：为处理“共享前缀、不同分支”的偏好差异，引入混合优势估计（global advantage + expert-tree internal advantage），并通过 advantage blocking 解决共享前缀上的梯度冲突，提升训练稳定性；同时采用 mix policy optimization（含 off-policy shape）在混合经验上更新策略。论文还给出从专家前缀分支探索优于纯自探索的理论论证（附录E），并用熵与奖励方差实证支持（Figure 4）。","experiments":"作者通过现象分析展示两类基线缺陷：Zero-RL 早期生成有效代码/动作困难且易进入 react mode；SFT+RL 存在分布迁移适应期、后期低熵坍塌与能力僵化。E3-TIR 在使用 <10% 合成数据的情况下优于 LLMs can reproduce insecure coding patterns from training data. Many security-hardening adaptations rely almost exclusively on supervision from the final transformer layer, creating a “final-layer bottleneck”: vulnerability-discriminative cues are distributed across layers and become less separable near the output representations optimized for next-token prediction.","importance":"With code LLMs widely used in real development, insecure generations can propagate vulnerabilities into the software ecosystem, and developers often miss these flaws. The paper identifies a concrete architectural/supervision mismatch (final-layer-only) and proposes a practical remedy that improves security while preserving functional correctness and keeping inference overhead low.","technical_approach":"DeepGuard is a hybrid framework combining training-time adaptation and lightweight inference-time steering.\n1) Diagnosis: layer-wise linear probing shows vulnerability signals are most detectable in intermediate-to-upper layers and attenuate toward the final layers (Figure 1).\n2) Multi-layer semantic aggregation: an attention-based aggregator dynamically fuses hidden states from multiple upper layers to produce an aggregated representation more sensitive to security cues (Figure 2B).\n3) Security analyzer + multi-objective training: the aggregated representation feeds a dedicated security analyzer; LoRA-based adaptation is trained with objectives that jointly optimize security improvement and functional correctness.\n4) Inference steering: compute a prompt-conditioned, context-aware security bias once and apply it to logits during generation, avoiding per-step re-evaluation overhead.","experiments":"Evaluated on five strong code LLMs for both security and functional correctness. On Qwen2.5-Coder-3B, SVEN achieves sec-pass@1 of 70.47%; DeepGuard raises it to 80.76% while keeping pass@1 at 86.65% (close to the original model). Across models, DeepGuard improves the secure-and-correct metric by 11.9% on average over SVEN, and shows generalization to vulnerability types held out during training.","reading_guide":"$5d","authors_note":"The authors’ thesis is that security-relevant signals are not concentrated in the final layer; final-layer-only supervision misses discriminative information present in intermediate/upper layers. DeepGuard explicitly aggregates cross-layer cues, trains with security–correctness co-optimization, and adds a deployable, low-overhead inference-time logit bias computed once from the prompt."},"reading_tier":"skim","recommendation":{"zh":"“final-layer 做安全监督”这个默认做法被点名不干净，值得看其多层聚合带来的可分性提升是否真不伤功能；重点读表示分析图和与常规对齐的对照实验。","en":"It challenges the common “final-layer-only” safety supervision assumption; worth checking whether multi-layer aggregation truly improves separability without hurting utility—focus on the representation analysis and the head-to-head baselines."}},{"id":"2604.09107","title":"TensorHub: Scalable and Elastic Weight Transfer for LLM RL 强化学习（RL）训练中，trainer 高频产出新权重、海量 rollout worker 频繁拉取权重，权重传输成为系统瓶颈。现有方案要么依赖静态通信组（如 NCCL）难以应对弹性/故障；要么点对点扇出导致拥塞（如 UCX）；要么通过分布式存储实现解耦但引入“push 到存储 + pull 到 worker”的双倍数据搬运与巨大存储开销，尤其在 TB 级权重下不可承受。","importance":"权重传输效率直接决定 RL 训练吞吐、GPU stall 时间与可扩展性，也决定能否利用异构/弹性资源（如 spot GPU、跨数据中心）。论文提出一种能同时兼顾“存储接口的解耦灵活性”和“直接传输的高效率”的新抽象，对大规模生产 RL 训练具有直接工程价值。","technical_approach":"提出 Reference-Oriented Storage（ROS）与其生产系统实现 TensorHub。\n1) 核心抽象（ROS）：对上层呈现“权重版本像存储在系统里、可按需 fetch”的接口；但底层不实际存任何权重副本，而是追踪哪些 rollout worker 的 GPU 上已经持有该不可变版本权重，并直接从这些 in-place 副本服务读取请求，从而避免额外拷贝与双倍搬运。\n2) 关键机制：\n- Mutability 之上提供拓扑感知调度、流水线式复制以扩展吞吐；为模型并行组提供强一致视图；具备故障检测与恢复编排，支持动态扩缩容与多数据中心场景。","experiments":"在数十到上千 GPU 的 RL 工作负载、带 spot churn 的弹性集群、以及跨数据中心拓扑上评估。\n- 1024 GPU 训练任务：相比 NCCL，总 GPU stall time 最多降低 6.7×。\n- 弹性集群：相比 Weight transfer becomes a major bottleneck. Existing approaches either rely on static collectives (e.g., NCCL) that are brittle under failures and elasticity, use point-to-point fan-out (e.g., UCX) that suffers contention, or use storage-based decoupling that doubles data movement (push to storage then pull to workers) and incurs prohibitive space overhead for TB-scale weights.","importance":"Weight transfer efficiency directly impacts RL throughput, GPU stall time, and the ability to exploit heterogeneous/elastic resources (spot GPUs) and multi-datacenter setups. The paper proposes a new abstraction that preserves the flexibility of a storage interface while approaching the efficiency of direct transfers, with clear production relevance.","technical_approach":"The paper introduces Reference-Oriented Storage (ROS) and its production system TensorHub.\n1) ROS abstraction: exposes the illusion that weight versions are stored and can be fetched on demand, but physically stores no copies. Instead, it tracks which workers already hold immutable weight versions on GPUs for inference and serves reads directly from these in-place replicas, avoiding extra copies and the push-then-pull overhead.\n2) Key mechanisms:\n- Mutability contract: constrains mutation/buffer-reuse semantics so reads remain safe and version-correct.\n- Retention protocol: specifies which versions must be kept; in corner cases where a version may be lost, it offloads a copy to CPU memory to ensure availability.\n3) TensorHub engineering: topology-aware scheduling, pipelined replication for throughput scaling, strong consistency within model-parallel groups, and fault detection/recovery to support dynamic scaling and multi-datacenter operation.","experiments":"Evaluated on RL workloads from dozens to 1,000+ GPUs, elastic clusters with spot churn, and cross-datacenter topologies.\n- 1024-GPU task: up to 6.7× reduction in total GPU stall time vs NCCL.\n- Elastic cluster: 4.8× faster updates vs UCX via dynamic load balancing.\n- Cross-datacenter: 19× reduction in GPU stall time by avoiding redundant TCP transfers.\nAlso reported as deployed in ByteDance production for cutting-edge RL training.","reading_guide":"$5e","authors_note":"The central insight is that RL weight versions are immutable and already highly replicated on inference GPUs; these replicas can act as the storage substrate. agent 生态通过可安装技能扩展能力，技能包逐渐包含可学习权重（分类器/路由器/解析器等）。这使攻击面从“运行时上下文”转移到“安装时工件（artifact）”，形成供应链后门：即使网关 LLM、解析器、外部输入都做了防护，技能内部模型仍可在执行路径中触发恶意行为。论文强调该风险与传统 NLP 后门不同：触发器往往是多个字段的合取（compositional triggers）、字段本身看似无害且是结构化参数，导致检测更难、误报代价更高。","technical_approach":"BadSkill 将攻击落在“技能内置分类器”上：攻击者发布一个看似良性的技能，其内部调用的模型 fθ 被后门微调，使其在常规参数空间中学习到“语义触发组合→恶意决策”的映射。方法层面强调三点：\n1) 触发器表达：不依赖单 token 或显眼字符串，而是利用技能调用的多字段参数（如任务类型/选项/目标/格式等）构造语义组合触发；单个字段独立看正常，但组合满足时触发。\n2) 训练策略：使用复合训练目标（composite objective），在保证正常功能（benign-side behavior）不显著退化的同时，提高触发条件下的攻击成功率（ASR）。论文摘要与引言提到结合“语义组合触发 + hard negatives + 复合目标”，其中 hard negatives 用于压制模型对“部分触发/近似触发”的误触发，迫使模型学习合取逻辑。\n3) 系统落地：在一个轻量 OpenClaw-inspired 的技能执行模拟环境中实现端到端链路（网关路由→技能加载→参数解析→技能内模型调用），强调攻击不依赖特定框架细节，而是泛化到“任何捆绑模型的技能工件”。","experiments":"论文在模拟技能环境中做案例评估：覆盖 8 种模型架构（约 494M–7.1B，来自 5 个模型家族）与 8 类可触发技能类别。主要结果包括：\n- 攻击有效性：在 8 个触发技能上平均 ASR 最高可达 消融、扰动鲁棒性表：用于判断攻击是否“高效且隐蔽”。\n- 创新点抓手：\n  - 将后门从“模型服务端/训练数据”迁移到“可安装技能工件中的内置模型”，并强调供应链属性。\n  - 触发器从单点 token 变为结构化参数的语义合取，并用 hard negatives 强化合取学习。\n  - 在技能执行栈中做端到端评估，而非仅离线分类器指标。\n\nskim（泛读建议：快速把握贡献）\n- Sun"],"notable_authors":[],"tags":["agent-security","backdoor-attack","supply-chain","tool-ecosystem","poisoning"],"links":{"arxiv":"https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09378","pdf":"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.09378","github":null,"project":null,"source_url":null}},"summary_en":{"core_problem":"The paper studies a supply-chain threat in agent skill ecosystems that is not captured by prompt injection or ordinary tool misuse: a third-party skill can bundle a learned model artifact (model-in-skill) whose weights are backdoor-tuned to execute a hidden payload only when structured skill parameters satisfy attacker-chosen semantic trigger combinations. Because the malicious logic lives in opaque model parameters rather than explicit code branches, conventional code review and input sanitization provide limited protection.","importance":"As agents become extensible via installable skills, skills increasingly ship with learned components (classifiers/routers/parsers). This shifts the security boundary to the installed artifact: even if the gateway LLM, parsers, and external inputs are hardened, an embedded model can still implement trigger-conditioned behavior inside the skill’s execution path. The setting differs from classic NLP backdoors because triggers are often conjunctions over multiple individually benign structured fields, making detection harder and increasing the cost of false positives.","technical_approach":"BadSkill instantiates the attack by embedding a backdoored classifier inside an ostensibly benign skill. The embedded model fθ is fine-tuned so that routine structured parameters encode a semantic, compositional trigger: each field looks normal in isolation, but their combination activates the payload. The approach emphasizes: (1) semantic compositional triggers over structured parameters rather than single-token cues; (2) a composite training objective that jointly preserves benign behavior while maximizing trigger-time attack success; and (3) hard negatives to suppress partial/near-trigger activations, encouraging true conjunctive trigger learning. The attack is evaluated end-to-end in a lightweight OpenClaw-inspired simulation that preserves gateway routing, skill loading, parsing, and runtime model invocation.","experiments":"In the simulated skill environment, the authors evaluate across eight model architectures (~494M–7.1B parameters) spanning five model families and eight triggerable skill categories. Key findings: (i) up to 99.5% average ASR across the eight triggered skills; (ii) strong poison-rate efficiency (high ASR at low poisoning rates; see the experiment curves for exact tradeoffs); and (iii) robustness under five types of text perturbations, suggesting the trigger is not a brittle surface pattern but more semantic/compositional.","reading_guide":"$5f","authors_note":"The authors’ main message is that agent security must consider the installed skill artifact itself: bundled model weights can carry stealthy, trigger-conditioned policies even when prompt-level defenses are in place. skills."},"reading_tier":"skim","recommendation":{"zh":"把 agent 供应链风险从“提示/工具”推进到“skill 内置小模型权重”，这个威胁面需要你更新审计动作：安装时做 artifact 扫描而非只做运行时防护；主要看触发器构造与检测失败案例。","en":"It moves agent supply-chain risk from prompts/tools to weights inside skills, implying a concrete audit shift: scan artifacts at install-time, not just runtime defenses; focus on trigger construction and detection-failure case studies."}},{"id":"2604.08844","title":"Spectral Geometry of LoRA Adapters Encodes Training Objective and Predicts Harmful Compliance","starred":false,"priority":"p2","source":"arxiv","sources":["arxiv"],"published_at":"2026-04-10T00:53:30+00:00","category_id":"post_train","cover_url":"/covers/2604_08844.png","hf_upvotes":0,"arxiv_categories":["cs.LG"],"summary":{"core_problem":"论文探讨一个“无需跑推理、只看权重”的问题：LoRA 微调产生的权重增量（ΔW）在谱几何（spectral geometry）上是否能识别微调目标（objective fingerprinting），并且这种几何信号是否能预测下游有害行为（harmful compliance）。更具体地：能否区分同一训练方法（DPO）下不同的目标（如反转 harmlessness vs 反转 helpfulness），以及这种区分是否与攻击成功率相关。","importance":"LoRA 让微调成本极低，也让“轻量但危险”的对齐破坏更易发生；而传统行为评测昂贵、慢、可被对抗、且可能无法访问推理接口。若能从适配器权重本身推断训练目标与风险，就能形成一种更可扩展的供应链/部署前审计手段（weight-space monitoring），用于检测被恶意或不当目标微调的适配器。","technical_approach":"作者在 Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct 上预注册实验，制造 38 个 LoRA 适配器，覆盖四类：健康 SFT 基线、DPO 反转 harmlessness、DPO 反转 helpfulness、以及 activation-steering 派生适配器。对每个 adapter、每层、每个模块（q_proj 与 v_proj）计算 LoRA 乘积 ΔW = BA，并做 SVD（ΔW=UΣVᵀ），提取三类特征：\n1) 幅值（magnitude）：Frobenius norm、spectral norm、top-k 奇异值等。\n2) 形状（shape）：stable rank、奇异值熵、有效秩、top-1 方差占比等。\n3) 方向（direction）：关键新增——与“健康适配器质心（healthy centroid）”的奇异向量余弦对齐（singular-vector cosine alignment）。\n将所有层/模块特征拼接成向量，用简单的 logistic regression 做分类与漂移检测。进一步用 PCA 分析扁平化 ΔW 的主轴，研究“目标差异”和“训练强度”在几何空间中的相对关系，并做模块级诊断（q_proj vs v_proj）。","experiments":"主要实验结论（按论文摘要给出的硬结果）：\n- 目标指纹识别：在同一训练方法 DPO 内，基于谱特征的逻辑回归在二分类漂移检测、以及所有 6 组 pairwise objective 对比上达到 AUC=1.00（N=38，预注册）。\n- 主轴分解：PCA 显示训练目标是最大变异轴（PC1），训练强度是次轴（PC2），且二者近似正交（与作者先验预期不同）。\n- 模块专门化：最难区分（反转 harmlessness vs 反转 helpfulness）时，q_proj 特征接近随机（AUC≈0.50），v_proj 可到 0.83；合并后达 1.00，提示诊断信号集中在 value 投影。\n- 跨方法失败与“系统性反转”：用 DPO 训练的分类器去判别 steering 制造的适配器时出现 AUC=0.00（不是噪声而是方向相反的系统性几何差异）。\n- 几何-行为关联：在 DPO 反转 harmlessness 条件下，权重漂移概率与 HEx-PHI 攻击成功率相关 ρ=0.72（N=24，p<0.001），且同类型内呈剂量-反应关系 ρ=0.986。\n- paper asks whether LoRA weight deltas contain a spectral-geometric fingerprint of the fine-tuning objective (not just that fine-tuning occurred), and whether that weight-space signal predicts downstream harmful compliance. Concretely: can we distinguish objectives within the same training method (DPO), such as inverted harmlessness vs inverted helpfulness, using weight-only features—without running inference?","importance":"LoRA makes fine-tuning cheap and widely accessible, which also lowers the barrier for misalignment and adversarial customization. Behavioral evaluations are costly, slow, and gameable, and may be infeasible when inference access is restricted. A reliable weight-only auditing signal would enable scalable supply-chain and pre-deployment screening of adapters for risky objectives.","technical_approach":"In a pre-registered study on Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct, the authors manufacture 38 LoRA adapters across four categories: healthy SFT baselines, DPO with inverted harmlessness preferences, DPO with inverted helpfulness preferences, and activation-steering-derived adapters. For each adapter, layer, and module (q_proj, v_proj), they compute the LoRA product ΔW = BA and perform SVD (ΔW=UΣVᵀ). They extract: (1) magnitude features (Frobenius/spectral norms, top-k singular values), (2) shape features (stable rank, singular-value entropy, effective rank, top-1 concentration), and (3) direction features—crucially, cosine alignment of singular vectors to a “healthy centroid” adapter.
